Important News Two

Central Party Headquarters and National Government Memorial Week 47

At 9:00 AM on the morning of March 2nd, the Central Party Headquarters held the 101st Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Central Committee members Dai Chuanxian, Ye Chucang, Yu Jingtang, Ma Chaojun, Miao Peicheng, Shao Yuanchong, Chen Lifu, Li Shizeng, Liu Luyin, Kong Xiangxi, and Ding Weifen, as well as guests from various agencies and staff members of the Party Headquarters, totaling over 400 people, attended. Dai Chuanxian presided over the meeting. After paying respects, the chairman reported, in brief, that since the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee resolved to convene a National Assembly, the Central Government has been working hard to prepare and has promulgated the Organic Law of the National Assembly. Because of his school commitments, he requested leave to go to Guangdong. During this period, the Central Government announced that he and Comrade Sun Ke would be responsible for the preparatory election headquarters. Because he had no experience, he did not know how to handle it and telegraphed the Central Government to appoint someone else, but the request was not approved. After returning to Nanjing, he had to work hard with Comrade Sun to take on the responsibility. He will take office in the National Government today and can report on the preparations for the National Assembly. As of last Friday, 18 election supervisors had taken office in 16 provinces and two cities. Within a few days, there should be continued reports of telegrams arriving in Nanjing. This shows that all regions are working hard. This meeting was short and preparations in various provinces were inevitably difficult, but the comrades in the local party headquarters worked hard to publicize and the government worked hard to prepare, which will ensure the meeting is held as scheduled. The main duties of the headquarters are to interpret laws and regulations. This has been handled by ten cadres appointed by the Central Government. Some of the cadres participated in drafting the laws and regulations, and some have worked in the Party Headquarters for a long time. There should be no difficulty in interpreting them. Next, the preparatory work for the meeting and reception is handled by the Fourth Group. The venue has been decided to borrow the newly built auditorium of the Central University. At that time, it will be completed as scheduled. The reception is also being planned carefully. The task of the National Assembly is what all comrades should pay special attention to. This issue is very important, and most people across the country still do not understand it, and many comrades in the Party Headquarters are still studying it. The full text of the Organic Law of the National Assembly explains the meaning of the National Assembly, saying that the National Government is following Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will to convene the National Assembly. This is the source of the meeting. According to this meaning, the task of the meeting is known. Foreign merchants often argue that Dr. Sun Yat-sen's reason for advocating the convening of the National Assembly was entirely to deal with the warlords Cao Kun and Wu Peifu. Now that the object has disappeared, it may not be necessary to convene it again. This argument is due to a lack of understanding of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings. Dr. Sun Yat-sen has specified two things in his speeches and declarations: (1) the unification of the country and (2) the construction of the country. How can unification be obtained and how can construction be done? These are the questions of the National Assembly itself. But before the meeting, there should be a correct concept, and then publicity can be carried out. Dr. Sun Yat-sen said that all construction should start with psychological construction and emphasized the swearing-in ceremony. The National Assembly has a short session, and national affairs are numerous and complex. The unification of military affairs, finance, internal affairs, and transportation all require concrete plans. All of these are specialized knowledge and cannot be determined in a short period of time by a collection of representatives who are not specialized scholars. Therefore, in order to seek unification, it is necessary to start with psychological construction first. In the past few years, our party has been working to eliminate reactionary warlords in order to build the Republic of China. But the construction of an official country requires the responsibility of all people in the country. To build, there must first be determination. This determination is the beginning of psychological construction. Therefore, the first task of the National Assembly is to convene national representatives in one hall to accept Dr. Sun Yat-sen's ideology, representing national citizens swearing that the national citizens believe in the Three Principles of the People and strive to build. Second, the path to construction has many threads, but the construction plan has been developed by Dr. Sun Yat-sen. For example, when we build a house, we must first have a blueprint. The engineer builds according to the blueprint and cannot change the blueprint. The things that have been decided in the blueprint are the blueprint for building the Republic of China, which is Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Outline of National Reconstruction. This is still a complete blueprint that must be followed. Until the completion of the tutelage, the Party will return the heavy responsibility it bears to the people. Before the people accept it, in other words, during the period of building the Republic of China, it should be carried out in accordance with this outline. Since the establishment of the National Government, it has been working wholeheartedly in accordance with the Outline of National Reconstruction. However, this kind of construction work requires not only the efforts of the comrades of the Party but also the concerted efforts of all the people of the country in order to succeed. Therefore, the National Assembly has another major task, which is for the representatives attending the meeting to represent the national people in accepting Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Outline of National Reconstruction. After the meeting, the national people trust the work of the Party and should also fulfill their respective obligations in accordance with the Outline. From the above, it can be seen that the task of the National Assembly is to have the national people clearly accept the Three Principles of the People in law, and to have the national people clearly recognize in law that the construction of the Republic of China should be carried out in accordance with the Outline of National Reconstruction. On these two points, during the period of national construction, there should be a covenant between the Party and the people. Dr. Sun Yat-sen gave several lectures in Japan on the matter of the provisional constitution. After the Xinhai Revolution, the format of European constitutions was imitated and a provisional constitution was promulgated, but this was not the provisional constitution that Dr. Sun Yat-sen hoped for. The provisional constitution advocated by Dr. Sun Yat-sen was the Party responsible for building the country and the people of the country agreeing on how to build the Republic of China and who should be given the power to build the country. Therefore, the meaning of the provisional constitution is roughly the same as the meaning of the three chapters of the provisional constitution in history and is very different from the meaning of the constitution. Before the foundation of the Republic of China is stable, if a provisional constitution that is the same as the constitution is formulated, the people are not prepared to implement the provisional constitution, and the government does not have the conditions to fulfill it, it will inevitably lead to mutual violations of the law. For more than ten years, the meaning of the provisional constitution and the constitution have often been confused. Dr. Sun Yat-sen has explained in detail the tasks that the people should bear in his Outline of National Reconstruction and his will. Therefore, if the National Assembly advocates a provisional constitution, the Party, in order to make the people understand the tasks that the people should bear during the period of national construction, can also advocate the formulation of a provisional constitution, but the meaning of the provisional constitution is only these points: (1) The Chinese Kuomintang, which bears political responsibility, and the people decide in law what methods to use during the period of national construction to fulfill the task of complying with the Outline of National Reconstruction. (2) Dr. Sun Yat-sen's advocacy is covered in the Three Principles of the People, the Outline of National Reconstruction, Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will, etc. There are many threads. How should the key points be extracted and the most important points that the Party and the people should jointly adhere to be simply stipulated so that there is something to follow in the future? Regarding the issue of the provisional constitution, a concerted effort should be made in publicity in the future so as not to confuse the meaning of the provisional constitution with the constitution. The Central Government has not yet made a formal decision on this matter. Today, the Central Standing Committee will have concrete and definite resolutions so that everyone has a basis. The Central Committee members who went to various places to inspect party affairs all have this idea, so I very much hope that the Central Standing Committee will have a concrete and detailed decision on this matter. I deeply feel that this issue is very important, so I will explain it based on Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings. I hope that everyone will seek a common point in their thoughts and wills, and then they can achieve good results, etc. After Dai's report, the ceremony was completed and the meeting adjourned. On the same morning at 10:00 AM, the National Government held Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week. Chiang Kai-shek, Yu Youren, Sun Ke, Dai Chuanxian, Song Ziwen, Kong Xiangxi, Zhu Peide, Cai Yuanpei, Wang Chonghui, Wang Boqun, Shao Yuanchong, Liu Shangqing, Chen Bulei, Chen Lifu, Cao Haosen, Jiang E, Chen Shaokuan, Zhang Huichang, Wang Zhengting, Lin Xiang, Ru Yuli, Zhu Lihe, Chen Yi, and staff members from the civil service and military affairs departments of the National Government, totaling over 300 people, attended. Chiang Kai-shek presided over the meeting. After paying respects, Chiang reported on the issue of the provisional constitution, and then the ceremony was completed and the meeting adjourned.

The Waning Bandit Forces in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi 48

Hankou Correspondence: The largest military organizations of the bandits in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces are in four locations: the border area of Anhui, Henan, and Hubei; western Hubei and Hunan; the border area of Hunan and Jiangxi; and southern Jiangxi. Please allow me to explain them separately.

The bandit army in the border area of Anhui, Henan, and Hubei consists of the Fourth, Eighth, and newly organized Twentieth Armies of the Red Army, with over 20,000 soldiers and nearly 40,000 Red Guards. Led by Li Can, the pseudo-commander of the Eighth Army, they are based north of Huang'an and Macheng and have established a Soviet government. All bandits who murder and steal, as well as defeated soldiers and vagrants, raise the red flag and unite with them. In each battle, they drive the Red Guards, who are poorly equipped and untrained, to harass our army's front lines, while their main force, the Red Army, hides in a corner, specializing in attacking our army's weaknesses. They have repeatedly engaged in fierce battles with Xia Douyin's Thirteenth Army and Zhang Yinxiang's division, commanded by Ji Hongchang. Their goal is to seize Huangma to remotely support the Jiangxi bandits. Our army has been besieging them for a long time. The reasons for this are fivefold: (1) Accumulated snow blocks the roads, making transportation difficult and inflexible. The bandit army burns all rice and firewood that they cannot carry when they retreat, leaving us with nothing to take. (2) The bandits use the border of Anhui and Henan as a retreat, appearing and disappearing unpredictably, making it difficult for us to pursue them. (3) The reconnaissance of the bandit situation is inaccurate, often mistaking the Red Guards for the Red Army and focusing our efforts on dealing with them, losing sight of the location of the main Red Army, which they then exploit. (4) The people are afraid of the bandits' burning and killing, and they bow their heads and dare not reveal the bandit situation. (5) Each army divides the pacification area, only driving the bandits out of the territory, and cannot cooperate fully to achieve the effect of encirclement and suppression. Now, the headquarters and the border defense offices of Hubei, Anhui, and Henan have formulated a new plan to target the Red Army with the means of "catching the thief, catch the king" and severely attack them. The armies are united, without dividing boundaries, with the goal of eliminating the bandits as the achievement, not just driving them away. On one hand, various cleansing bureaus are established to strengthen the local defense forces, enabling them to guard and allowing the army to eliminate the bandits' strength. The bandit army, having been severely attacked by the Thirteenth Army, has fled from northern Macheng into Henan Province. However, their remnants are still hidden among the bushes and are determined to be cleared within one month starting from March 1.

Western Hubei and Hunan: The bandits in western Hubei and Hunan use Honghu as their nest. After our army destroyed Honghu, the bandits fled to Jianshi and the Hua'an area of Hunan, spreading like wildfire and meeting with He Long's remnants. Therefore, Xu Yuanquan, the border defense commander of Sichuan, Hunan, and Hubei, suggested that in the future, it is not necessary to break the bandit nest first, but to use the plan of encirclement and annihilation. He Long's bandits have a long history in the border of the three provinces. At first, they may not have been communists, but they changed their loyalty so many times that no one dared to comfort them. Having nowhere else to turn, they willingly attached themselves to the Red Army. However, they cannot get along with Zhu De and Mao Zedong. If He Long is pursued relentlessly by the government army, he will inevitably disperse his followers and take a few confidants in disguise to escape. Before long, he will return and regroup his remaining followers. The unemployed and desperate people of Sangzhi are numerous, and joining the bandits is their only means of survival. If forced, they will hide their guns and remain as ignorant people, enough to escape the eyes and ears of government soldiers. This is how He Long can gather and disperse his followers, but his strength is still very weak, with only five or six thousand guns. The organization of the so-called Red Guards is far inferior to other communist bandits. They have now fled north to the Hefeng area and are being cleared by Xu Yuanquan's division, a part of Liu Xiang's Sichuan army, and the Hunan armies of Li Jue, Chen Quzhen, and Zhang Ying. The government has ordered Ye Kaixin, the former commander of the Eighth Army, to be the border defense commander of Hunan and Guizhou to prevent them from fleeing south. However, few people know the whereabouts of He Long himself.

The border area of Hunan and Jiangxi: The border area of Hunan and Jiangxi is bounded by Pingliu in Hunan and Xiutong in Jiangxi. Peng Dehuai, the communist leader who attacked Changsha previously, used this as his base. The communists previously planned not to seize cities but to take the first step of communizing the border towns. The earliest attempt was in the four towns on the border of Hunan and Jiangxi, so the four towns have been a bandit den for many years, and the people have a tendency to be communist. After Peng Dehuai and Huang Gonglue went south to join Zhu De and Mao Zedong, Kong Hechong took over the area and is now entrenched in the Qinglin secluded area under the jurisdiction of Xiushui County with 10,000 guns. Kong's goal is to follow in the footsteps of Peng Dehuai and Huang Gonglue and attack Changsha, creating a second great terror. However, He Jian did his best to defend the border, and Kong could not succeed, so he changed to defending his position, attempting to contain our military strength. However, our side also detected that Kong's bandits were becoming increasingly poor, so they ordered the original Eighteenth and Fiftieth Divisions of Jiangxi Province and the three divisions of Wang Dongyuan, Peng Weiren, and Chen Guangzhong of the Pingliu Hunan Army, as well as the Guo Huazong Division under Wang Jinyu of Pingxiang, to form a joint defense and transfer a large part of the army to suppress southern Jiangxi. At this time, they are not anxious to eliminate Kong's bandits, but to block their way out, so that they become trapped.

Southern Jiangxi: Ganzhou is where the main bandit troops are located. Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Peng Dehuai, and Huang Gonglue are concentrated here, occupying Ningdu, Luokou, Guangchang, Dongbei, and Xingguo. Peng Dehuai and Huang Gonglue are at odds with Zhu De and Mao Zedong, but they have become inseparable and must consolidate their position in order to struggle. Because they have been fighting for thousands of miles and have suffered heavy losses, they are actively coercing the people to join and replenish their forces, and building fortifications to defend against government troops without the intention of moving far away. The government army has not actively advanced for the following reasons: (1) In view of the previous failures, they will not advance lightly until each army has reached the designated location and obtained reliable communication. (2) They fear that a hasty attack will cause the bandits to flee elsewhere, hindering the annihilation. (3) The areas of central Jiangxi are covered with thorns, and it is necessary to first weaken the bandits' wings before there are no worries. According to recent reports, there are occasional scattered bandits harassing west of Xingguo, seemingly coveting Ganzhou. However, these troops are scattered and unable to withstand a single blow. Considering the past, the communist bandits are accustomed to using strategies of leaving a voice and visiting the west. Gu Wenchang responded to Ying Fen's visit to his private residence at around 11:00. Yang Yuebin has been harassing Nanfeng and Lichuan in the east. How do we know that the bandits are not deliberately creating suspicion to confuse our army's vision and then sneak into Fujian through a side road? Fortunately, the anti-bandit authorities are paying attention to this (February 28).

He Yingqin Reports on the Bandit-Communist Situation in Four Provinces 49

▲At the Weekly Memorial Ceremony in the Nanchang Headquarters

Nanchang Correspondence: Yesterday, at the weekly memorial ceremony for the Commander-in-Chief held at the Nanchang Headquarters, He Yingqin reported on the situation of the bandit-communist groups Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Peng Dehuai, Huang Gonglue, Kong Hechong, Li Wenlin, He Long, Kuang Jixun, Fang Zhimin, Shao Shiping, as well as Li Mingrui in the four provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Fujian. He also urged the various departments to strictly guard military secrets and protect the people. The general gist is as follows: "Fellow comrades, upon the orders of the Commander-in-Chief, we have come to Jiangxi to handle the military affairs of suppressing the bandits. We have been in Nanchang for three weeks now. During this period, on the one hand, we have been investigating the situation of the communist bandits and planning a strict method of extermination. On the other hand, we have been concentrating and strengthening our forces from all directions, hoping to capture them all in one fell swoop without letting anyone escape. Now, the various armies are actively proceeding according to the predetermined plan. Today, taking advantage of the opportunity of the weekly memorial ceremony, I will report to you on the bandit situation in various aspects. (1) In the southern Jiangxi area, the major bandit groups of Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Peng Dehuai, and Huang Gonglue, claiming to number tens of thousands, in reality have no more than twenty thousand bandits. Most of the rest are coerced peasants, the so-called Red Guards by the bandits. They are now entrenched in Ningdu, Guangchang, Huangpi, Xiaobulekou, Donggu, Futian, Longgangxu, Pitou, and other places, all of which are currently under our military surveillance. It will not be difficult to gradually eliminate them with the advance of our main forces. (2) In eastern Jiangxi, the groups of Fang Zhimin, Shao Shiping, and Zhou Jianping took advantage of the emptiness of our Yushan defenses to seize Yushan. After our troops rushed to suppress them, they were defeated and fled into Mopan Mountain. Our Ruan division once defeated these bandits near Gangkou, capturing many of them. They are currently being searched and suppressed by separate routes. (3) In western Jiangxi, the groups of Kong Hechong and Li Wenlin are entrenched in the area of Maxu, Youju, and Tonggu Tieshuguan under the jurisdiction of Xiushui. Our Fifth Route Army has contacted the various units in eastern Hunan to carry out encirclement and suppression. They will be eliminated soon. As for the small groups of communist bandits in the areas of Xiajiang, Anfu, and Lianhua, who collude with local peasant bandits and occasionally create disturbances, they have been successively dispersed by our army and are being gradually eliminated. As for the bandits of Longgang Yanxia, who were previously dispersed by the Hao division, in order to prevent a resurgence, Commander Hao has been ordered to continue his efforts to suppress them. (4) In eastern and southern Hunan, the major bandit groups that originally existed have long been defeated by our army. Now, although there are scattered bandit groups in Zhangjiafang, Xiaohe, Dindushi, Fenglin, Cenchuan, Nanjiang in the Pingliu area, and Gaolong and Yanfang in the Chayou area, they are not a major threat. They are currently being suppressed by Commander Liu, while the military department is assisting in the establishment of people's self-defense organizations in order to eliminate the bandits in various areas. (5) In western Hunan and western Hubei, the main force of the He Long bandits originally had two to three thousand guns. After our armies in western Hubei, northern Hunan, and eastern Sichuan jointly suppressed them, these bandits have been repeatedly defeated. Now, in Shinan and Hefeng, there are fewer than a thousand guns left. It will not be difficult to exterminate them with one encirclement and attack. (6) The bandits on the border of Anhui and Hubei have been vigorously pursued and suppressed by General Commander Ji in connection with the units in eastern Anhui and northern Hubei. The bandit forces are extremely weak and easy to eliminate. As for Li Mingrui's unit, after being blocked and suppressed by our Eighth Route Army, their strength has been greatly reduced. They now have only three to four hundred guns. Although they have fled separately through Nongjiang in southern Hunan and Chongyi in southern Jiangxi, our Nineteenth Route Army is blocking them in front, and the Duan department of the Fourth Route Army is chasing them from behind. It will not be long before these bandits are completely annihilated.

Judging from the situation in various aspects, although the areas where the communist bandits have spread seem to be very wide, in terms of real strength, they are not many. And although they claim to be so-and-so army and so-and-so division, and hang up a communist sign, in reality they do everything from murder and arson to rape and plunder. They are completely more dangerous than the previous bandits and bandits. They are nothing more than extremely evil bandits and bandits. Although the masses, under their brutality, temporarily endure suffering and follow them, once the national army arrives, after propaganda and persuasion, who would not want to abandon the darkness and turn to the light and repeat their peaceful and prosperous life? Therefore, we believe that once the suppression order is issued, the communist bandits, no matter how cunning, will not be difficult to wipe out in one fell swoop. However, in the areas where the communist bandits are entrenched, the masses have been deeply poisoned and suffered the most severely. In the future, after the military victory is achieved, we hope that the comrades in the party and government will work hard to fundamentally seek a method of rectification and rehabilitation, so that the masses in the bandit areas can be thoroughly cleared of the abyss of suffering and placed in a peaceful life.

Regarding this bandit suppression, we should pay attention to several special matters: (1) Military secrets should be absolutely protected. The most important thing in using troops is to know yourself and your enemy. Therefore, we should do our best to detect the situation of the bandits, but our own situation must not be made known to others. All our military plans, as well as the deployment of troops and the location of troops, have an absolutely secret nature. We must strictly prevent leakage or inadvertently publishing them in newspapers. Our comrades must understand the danger of leaking military secrets and take the protection of military secrets as their most important responsibility. (2) We should focus on fundamentally eliminating the communist bandits and not seek quick results in terms of the situation. In this bandit suppression, we must recognize that the Communist Party is the biggest obstacle to the National Revolution, that is, the biggest enemy of the Chinese people. We must use meticulous plans and preparations to fundamentally eliminate them. We are not satisfied with being able to recover a certain place in a month or half a month. We must accomplish the task of eliminating the bandit leaders, confiscating firearms, and pacifying the people before we can be considered to have achieved our task. (3) The bandit situation should be reported in a realistic manner. Since we have embraced the determination to fundamentally eliminate the communist bandits and have a fundamental plan for elimination, once the suppression order is issued, we will inevitably achieve success step by step day by day. (4) The people should be effectively protected. The army's suppression of bandits is aimed at seeking the well-being of the people. Therefore, it is appropriate to strictly abide by discipline, cherish the people, and absolutely not disturb the people. (5) Give the oppressed people a chance to reform. A general group of people were coerced into joining the communist bandits. We should treat those who were coerced without discrimination and give them a way to reform. Communist Party members who surrender themselves are especially welcome." (February 25th)

Huang Shaoxiong Arrives in Guangzhou to Discuss Guangxi Affairs 50

▲Huang Plans Three Post-Guangxi Rehabilitation Plans

Guangzhou Correspondence: The newly appointed Post-Guangxi Rehabilitation Supervisor Huang Shaoxiong, after arriving in Hong Kong from Shanghai on the 21st, and eager to resolve the Guangxi issue, took the night boat from Hong Kong to Guangzhou on the 23rd. He arrived at about 7:00 am on the 24th. Those traveling with him included Gong Jieyuan, Lü Jingqiu, Huang Weifang, Huang Fang, and more than a dozen staff members. Those from the political circles who welcomed him at the pier included Deng Yanhua, Director of the Department of Construction, Ouyang Ju, Director of the Public Security Bureau, and the head of the Eighth Route Army Headquarters, and several dozens more. After Huang stepped ashore, he shook hands with the welcomers and exchanged brief greetings. Then, he took a car with Deng Yanhua and two others to the Tuisiyuan Garden in Dongshan to visit Chen Mingshu, Chairman of the Provincial Government, for a long talk. Then, he mixed with a small number of old acquaintances to Tuisiyuan for lunch. After lunch, he went to Central Park with Chen Ce and several other former ball partners to play velvet ball to pass the time. In the evening, Chen Mingshu hosted a banquet at Tuisiyuan for Huang. Those accompanying him included senior officers of the headquarters and members of the provincial government and directors of various departments. It was not until 5:00 pm that the banquet ended. According to Huang, those who visited him said that he would handle the Guangxi situation in accordance with the central government's intentions. In the future, the downsizing of the Guangxi army will be allocated about 2 million yuan by the central government as demobilization expenses. It has been decided to abolish the division and brigade system of the Guangxi army. The whole of Guangxi will be divided into several defense zones with the establishment of garrison commands to engage in bandit suppression in order to seek local construction. According to Gong Jieyuan, a close confidant of Huang, Huang's plan for handling the aftermath of Guangxi province is: the first step is to divide the garrison areas and distribute troops to each area so as to engage in training; the second step is to conduct searches and suppress bandits and communist bandits; the third step is to organize the Guangxi Provincial Government. Zhang and the Guangxi army currently have about 20 regiments. In the future, the Post-Rehabilitation Supervision Office may be located in Nanning. According to Chen Shi (Chief Counselor of the Headquarters), who brokered the Guangxi peace talks, the central government will allocate about 1.6 to 1.8 million yuan to Guangxi province in installments. All matters concerning the reorganization of Zhang and the Guangxi army will be presided over by Huang Shaoxiong. In the future, it may be reorganized into three divisions. If Li Zongren, Zhang Fakui, Bai Chongxi and others decide to step down, the central government will give them titles and provide them with overseas expenses. If Li, Zhang, Bai, etc., actually step down and Supervisor Huang officially takes office, then the Eighth Route Army can withdraw from Wuzhou. (Evening of February 24th)

Eighth Route Army Stationed in Guangxi Withdraws Steadily 51

▲Eighth Route Army Between Guixian and Hengxian Has Completely Withdrawn

▲Fleet and Air Squadron Return to Guangdong in Succession

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Huang Shaoxiong arrived in Guangdong to discuss the post-Guangxi rehabilitation plan, the Eighth Route Army stationed in Guangxi has been returning to the north in succession. It is estimated that the troops that have been withdrawing in the past few days will have completed their departure. The 63rd Division's Huang Zhiwen Brigade arrived in Guangdong in succession yesterday and today. The Chen Hanguang Regiment of the Garrison Regiment on the Dahe side also departed from Guiping to the east on the afternoon of the 20th and arrived in Wuzhou on the 22nd to temporarily garrison in Wuzhou pending orders. At the same time, the 59th Division's Yu Hanmou Regiment, stationed on the Binjiang front, has also withdrawn to Guiping. According to a military officer who returned to Guangdong from Guangxi, there are no Eighth Route Army troops stationed between Guixian and Hengxian. Huang Renhuan's Brigade opened to the area between Tengxian and Guixian yesterday. Since there is no trace of the Eighth Route Army in Guixian, the first reserve hospital branch and the wounded soldier reception centers of various divisions and brigades were completely closed on February 10. All medicines, equipment, and wounded soldiers were transported to Wuzhou to join the personnel of the first hospital and moved to Guangdong in full. It is estimated that there are more than a hundred officers and soldiers and a large batch of medicines and equipment. On the evening of the 21st, they were transported to Guangdong in six civilian ships and sent to the General Army Hospital for disposal. As for the navy, the vessels stationed in Guangxi during the cessation of hostilities included the shallow-water gunboats Pingxi, Jingxi, Zhixin, Longxiang, and Lichen. They are now being withdrawn along with the army. The Zhixin, Longxiang, and Lichen vessels returned to the Guangdong River on the 22nd. The other Pingxi and Jingxi Southwest gunboats were seized from the Guangxi army during the war. The authorities plan to return them to the Guangxi Post-Rehabilitation Supervision Office for takeover. The air squadron of the Eighth Route Army Aviation Office originally had three aircraft in the first squadron, leaving three aircraft in Wuzhou. There was also a small squadron of aircraft protection team stationed at the airport. On the 24th, the three aircraft had flown from Wuzhou to Guangdong. The staff of the squadron and the protection team also returned to Guangdong by boat on the 25th and transferred to the Guangsan train this morning. According to military sources, since the various units of the Eighth Route Army will soon return to Guangdong, the defense areas of each division should be designated in advance in order to be responsible for bandit suppression. It is now roughly planned that the 59th Division's Yu Hanmou Regiment will be stationed in the Xijiang Zhaoqing area, the 62nd Division's Xiang Hanping's regiment will be stationed in the Dongjiang Chaozhou Meizhou area, and the 63rd Division's Li Yangjing's regiment will be stationed in the Beijiang area. The Huang Renhuan Brigade of the Training Brigade and the Zhang Ruigui Brigade of the First Independent Brigade will be stationed in Huizhou and Shantou. The Chen Hanguang Regiment of the Garrison Regiment and the Li Zhiping Regiment of the Fourth Independent Regiment will be stationed in Qinlian. The Fan Dexing Regiment of the First Independent Regiment will be stationed in Zhongshan Shunde and the Li Jiezhizhi Regiment of the Second Independent Regiment will be stationed in Gaolei and the Fourth Independent Regiment will be stationed in Dongguan Shilong. As soon as the troops return to their defenses, they will begin their pacification work. (February 26th)

Taiyuan Correspondence: The Shanxi rehabilitation problem has recently been on the right track since the new military commanders and provincial government commissions took office one after another. Before leaving Bingzhou, the various generals had concrete discussions on the issue of demobilization expenses and garrisons. The 450,000 yuan of demobilization expenses that Shang Zhen brought back from Tianjin have been distributed in advance. In addition to actively raising funds from the Finance Department, it is said that the 2 million yuan borrowed by the Northeast will be transported to Bingzhou and distributed when the demobilization pain points of the various armies are verified. The garrison of each army is currently planned to remain as it is for the time being. After the three divisions of Song Zheyuan, Pang Bingxun, and Sun Dianying are demobilized and transferred to the Pinghan Line, the entire province will be divided into several pacification areas and distributed equally. The various military closure matters are currently planned to be handled by a military closure committee. The committee has been actively preparing for a very small scale. It is planned to draw from the headquarters and various related military agencies.

Feng Sizhi, Director of the Education Department, has returned to Bingzhou from his home and has also gone to the department to inspect. Bandit Atmosphere Revives in Baodugu 54

Jinan Correspondence: In the 12th year of the Republic of China, the giant bandit Sun Meiyao of Baodugu robbed a train in Lincheng and plundered passengers. It was a sensation that attracted attention both at home and abroad. Baodugu is located at the junction of the five counties of Lin, Tan, Fei, Teng, and Yi. The mountains and valleys are dangerous and secluded, and it has long been a nest for bandits. After Sun Meiyao was executed, his brother Mei Song (i.e., Sun Jingtai) still led the remaining bandits to occupy and cause trouble, which has not been suppressed. Last year, the authorities recruited him and reorganized him into the 27th Division. However, Sun's wild nature was difficult to tame, and he soon rebelled again. Now, his power is very strong, and the harassment is even worse than before. The nearby residents have suffered greatly. Sun's bandits also coveted Zaozhuang, which is rich and a major town in southern Shandong. On the 19th of this month, they suddenly sent dozens of bandits to attack Zaozhuang. Fortunately, the local militia fought bravely and repelled them. Chen Yaohan of the 26th Division has sent the 157th Regiment to Zaozhuang to take care of the situation. At the same time, Li Hanzhang, the brigade commander of the 85th Brigade stationed in Tengxian, also ordered the Hou Zhaolin Regiment stationed in Lincheng to make proper joint defenses with the regiment. Yesterday, the General Headquarters received a telegram from Division Commander Cao Fulin reporting as follows: (1) According to Li Brigade Commander Hanzhang's report, Hou Regiment Commander reported that after the 27th Division of Sun Meisong in Lincheng was defeated by the Central Army, the bandits still fled back to the Baodugu area north of Zaozhuang and carried out looting and killing. The Baodugu area has always been a bandit's nest. Local bandits have been recruited many times in the past, and there are many military uniforms. They often mix with soldiers, so the people cannot tell the truth from the fake. At 8:00 pm on the evening, dozens of bandits attacked Zaozhuang. Fortunately, the militia repelled them, etc. (2) According to Li Brigade Commander Hanzhang's telegram, due to the scattered remnants of Sun Meisong fleeing into the mountains, the local area has been unstable. Yesterday, Division Commander Chen Yaohan sent his 157th Regiment to Zaozhuang to take care of the situation and ordered his brigade stationed in Lincheng Hou Zhaolin Regiment to make proper joint defenses with it. Respectfully reported by Cao Fulin (February 27th)

Russian Bandits Attempt to Rob Shenyang HSBC Bank Unsuccessful 56

Shenyang Correspondence: At 4:00 am on February 26, five Russian bandits in a car suddenly broke into the HSBC Bank at the Sankong Road in the Shenyang Commercial Port Area from the east. Each held a handgun and first went to the staff dormitory, where they used ropes to tie up the bank's Chinese staff, including Chu Ji and others, and forced them to tell them the location of the money and wealth storage warehouse. The bank staff immediately replied that there was no money. The Russian bandits searched the savings room and asked Chu for the key to open the cabinet to retrieve the money. Chu replied that there were a total of three keys, which were divided among the German, French, and Chinese managers. The three of them are not currently living in the bank. Seeing that there was no way to do it, the Russian bandits used an axe to completely split open the three iron locks on the safe. Due to the lack of a key, they could not open the last steel door despite their best efforts to chop it open. Seeing that too much time had passed, the Russian bandits were afraid of being discovered outside, so they had to return to the dormitory and search for the money around the staff, losing more than 60 silver yuan in total, and then went out the door to get into the car and drove away. The bound employees of the bank bit the ropes and broke free with their mouths, rushing to the Commercial Port Public Security First Branch to report. After Zhao Guanru, director of the branch, led the police to pursue the Russian bandits, they were no longer to be found. A police post was originally set up in front of the bank. On the day of the incident, the police officer Liu, who was on duty, had entered the basement boiler room to warm up due to the late night and cold weather and was sleeping soundly, so he did not notice the robbery. After the fact, the first branch of the Commercial Port investigated the previous situation and detained Liu for dereliction of duty and awaited punishment. (February 26th)

Resolutions of the Jinpu Road Garrison Meeting 57

Xuzhou Correspondence: The Jinpu Road Garrison Meeting was held today (28th). Wang Jun had not yet returned to Xuzhou from inspecting the 12th Division of Jin Handing's troops in Haizhou, so he entrusted Zeng Wanzhong, the deputy division commander of the 7th Division, to represent the chairman. The meeting was held at 1:00 pm in the conference room of the Garrison Headquarters. Those present included Jiang Xiang, representing Wei Lihuang of the 45th Division, Cheng Zhongqing, representing Zhang Lisheng of the 2nd Cavalry Division, Sun Yixin, representing Chen Yaohan of the 26th Division, Wang Haoding, the third battalion commander of the Railway Artillery Corps, Mo Woru, the battalion commander of the First Battalion of the Central Military Police, Qiu Yude, the chief of staff of the Garrison Department, and Cao Youyi, the section chief. Those present were Chen Xueshun, the military and police inspector of Xuzhou, Shen Yuanzhen, the chief adjutant of the Garrison Department, Liu Xianzhong, the director of the Transportation Office, Zhou Lin, the director of the Military Law Office, and Qin Zhenfu, the recording secretary. The chairman reported on the significance of the meeting, saying that Commander Wang was ordered to be responsible for the garrison of the Jinpu Road, and the 45th Division, the 2nd Cavalry Division, and the 26th Division were also assigned the same task. It is necessary to discuss the planning of the defense zone and the important items of garrison. Then, the proposals were discussed, totaling seven items. (1) The Garrison Department submitted a plan for the southern section of the Jinpu Road and decided on the garrison to protect the road in each district. It was resolved to divide the Jinpu Road into four districts, namely, the Pubeng section, the Bingsu section, the Suten section, and the Linzao branch line, which will be responsible for the garrison of the 2nd Cavalry Division, the 45th Division, the 26th Division, and the 7th Division, respectively. The scope of the garrison will be handled in full compliance with the garrison regulations issued by the headquarters. (2) Cheng Zhongqing, Director of the 42nd Division, and Jiang Xiang, Section Chief of the 45th Division, proposed that the headquarters in Meng stipulate the road protection expenses for the garrison troops, and the Garrison Department should be requested to submit the case for review and approval. It was resolved to submit the case to the headquarters for review. (3) Section Chief Cao Youyi proposed that the task of checking and inspecting stations and vehicles on this road should be solely responsible for the military police in accordance with previous orders. It was resolved to follow the previous orders. (4) Battalion Commander Mo Woru of the Military Police Battalion proposed that the garrison troops should be issued armbands by the Garrison Department for identification. It was resolved that the armbands of the military police officers and soldiers should be manufactured and issued by the Garrison Department. (5) Section Chief Jiang Xiang of the 45th Division proposed that the officers and soldiers of the garrison troops who are traveling on duty should be issued travel permits by the Road Bureau. It was resolved that the Transportation Office of this headquarters should send a letter to the Road Bureau requesting that they be issued. (6) Battalion Commander Wang Haoding of the Armored Vehicle proposed that official telegrams of the garrison troops should be sent and received by the Road Bureau on their behalf in order to speed up the process. It was resolved that the Transportation Office of this headquarters should send a letter to the Road Bureau requesting that they be handled in accordance with this. (7) Director Cheng Zhongqing of the Cavalry Division proposed that the Road Station telephone should be used for emergency road garrison matters. It was resolved that the Transportation Office of the Garrison Department should refer to the successful case of the Jinghu Road and send a letter to the Road Bureau requesting that the Road Bureau inform the stations to allow the road protection troops to borrow them at any time. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 pm. The Garrison Headquarters immediately hosted a banquet at the Garden Hotel for all the representatives. The representatives have decided to return to their defenses on March 1 and report to their respective division commanders for compliance. (February 28th)

松江 58

Establishment of the Si Jing Town Chamber of Commerce: The preparatory work for the Si Jing Town Chamber of Commerce in this county has been underway for several months. Now, various industries in this town have legally organized twelve trade associations, including rice merchants, lumber merchants, general merchandise, sauce and fermented grain merchants, rice milling, silk and cloth, fresh meat, fresh eggs, imported goods, art materials, and pickled goods, to join the preparatory work. The drafted articles of association have been submitted to the County Reorganization Committee and the County Government for approval. The inaugural election meeting was held on February 9th of this year. The County Reorganization Committee sent Comrade Ye Guanqun to provide guidance, and the County Government sent Zhang Yunfeng, the patrol officer of this town, to supervise the election. A total of eighty-nine representatives attended. The election results selected Li Xiuzhe and fifteen others as executive committee members, Chen Wenguang and five others as alternate executives, Xu Shenxian and seven others as supervisory committee members, and Song Xingqing and three others as alternate supervisors. The next day, the executive committee members mutually elected Li Xiuzhe, Sheng Junchang, Shen Jun, Hu Sigai, and Qin Yusheng as standing committee members, with Li Xiuzhe as chairman. The matter was immediately reported to the County Reorganization Committee for record.

The Water Police Crack Down on Street Robbery: The merchants Zhang Zonghua and Zhang Dezhang of Xin Jie Town, Pudong, including six shops, namely Wan Yuan Dye House, Shou Chun Hua Store, and Sheng Shun De Zhu Xie Xing, were robbed at the end of last year, but the perpetrators have not yet been apprehended. Recently, the Waterborne Provincial Public Security Team discovered a suspicious Jiangbei boat passing by and ordered it to be inspected. They found robbers Zhou Xingtang and others and recovered the stolen goods, which were escorted to the County Government for interrogation. Now, the County Government has ordered Police Chief Dong Futang to summon Zhang Zonghua, Dezhang, and merchants Zhang Shouxian, Jin Peisheng, Sheng Nankang, and Zhu Bosheng to come to court on the 8th of this month to identify the suspects in order to reach a verdict.

Establishment of the Literacy Campaign Committee: This county has been ordered to organize a Literacy Campaign Committee and elect representatives from people's organizations according to regulations. However, since the people's organizations in this county have not yet been fully organized, there have been doubts about the election of representatives. A telegram has been sent to the Provincial Government for instructions. Subsequently, the Provincial Government instructed that representatives should be elected from well-organized groups, and that it is better to have fewer representatives than to include unqualified ones. County Magistrate Jin summoned Ni Shichang, the Director of the Education Bureau, Zhu Shourren, the Chief of the Social Education Section, Yu Yingsen, the Director of the County Agricultural Field, Zhu Tiexian and Zhang Binzhi from the County Party Headquarters, and Shen Benqian, the representative of the social education organization, to establish the Propaganda Committee and plan for the establishment of district branches, township branches, and neighborhood offices by the end of March. The County Government has issued orders to all district offices to comply.

The Bandit Suppression Commander Returns to His Post: Cao Pang, the commander of the 2nd Regiment of the Security Force, was previously ordered to serve as the Commander of the Songhu Pacification Division. Recently, he was also ordered to serve concurrently as the Temporary Commander of Bandit Suppression in Songjinjiaping. He departed on the 22nd to search and suppress bandits in Punan for several days. As a result, more than a hundred suspected bandits were captured in Qianwei, Liujia Yanqiao, Xin Cang Yaqian, Xin Miao Sanqinggang, Jin Si Niangqiao, Jinshanwei, and other places. In addition, forty bandits were captured in Pinghu, Zhejiang, and were handed over to the Zhangyan Public Security Bureau to send personnel to escort them to the Pinghu County Government for investigation. The notorious bandits Ni A'gen (also known as Wu Baisheng), Guo A'xin, and Pan A'rong confessed without hesitation. They were executed by firing squad in Zhangyan yesterday as a warning.

Suzhou 59

Robbers Attempt to Rob Sauce Garden Unsuccessfully: In front of the Fu Cheng Sauce Garden on Da Ma Road outside Chang Gate, two robbers suddenly appeared at 9:30 pm (one day). One stood guard outside the counter, while the other took out a six-round pistol from his sleeve, entered the shop, and threatened to rob it. Fang Mingsheng, a shop assistant, bravely stepped forward, grabbed him around the waist, and pushed him outside the door. The two robbers then fled into the crowd.

City School Land Transferred to the Education Bureau for Management: The Suzhou Municipal Government abolished all city school land at the time, which was then taken over by the Finance Bureau. However, the Education Bureau believed that the city school land belonged to the education fund and should be managed by the Education Bureau. After repeated efforts, County Magistrate Huang ordered that the transfer be made after the end of the 19th year. Now that the winter grain tax collection has been completed, the Finance Bureau has transferred the field and house rental documents and the collected 6,869 yuan, 3 jiao, 2 fen, and 5 li to the Education Bureau yesterday (2nd).

Wuxi 60

Plainclothes Police Investigate Gambling, Causing Disturbances: On the evening of the day before yesterday (25th), at around 10 pm, dozens of people speaking in different accents, wearing plain clothes, and carrying guns suddenly arrived in Yangshuyuan Town, District 16 of Wuxi. They rushed to Zhang Shuntai's tobacco and paper shop on Zhongjie Street and broke open the door to search. Because the merchants and residents of the town had been robbed in previous years and had recently received extortion letters, they were like frightened birds. Upon hearing the alarming news, they suspected that a major disaster was coming and fled in panic. Later, after the Chamber of Commerce dispatched people to investigate, they learned that it was Han Weian, the official of the 14th Branch of the Zhangshe Public Security Bureau, leading the entire team to the town to investigate gambling. Because most of the police officers were in plain clothes, the merchants and residents did not understand the truth for a while and rushed to flee. The police officers suspected that they were gamblers and pulled people indiscriminately, almost causing a conflict. Fortunately, the Chamber of Commerce maintained order and no trouble occurred. Afterwards, all the merchants and residents of the town were extremely indignant that the police officers of the branch bureau had disturbed the public order by investigating gambling late at night. They unanimously joined together to file a complaint with the County Government and the Public Security Bureau, requesting a thorough investigation.

Recent Survey of Grain Storage: According to a recent survey, the data on the storage of rice, wheat, and miscellaneous grains in various warehouses in the county are as follows: 400,000 dan of japonica rice, 150,000 shi of brown japonica rice, 250,000 dan of indica rice (excluding accumulated grains), 33,000 shi of brown indica rice, 220,000 dan of round rice, 12,000 shi of brown round rice, 100,000 shi of wheat, 73,000 dan of soybeans, 26,000 dan of mung beans, 1,700 shi of cowpeas, 5,000 dan of barley, 3,200 shi of round wheat, 6,200 shi of corn, 1,500 shi of broad beans, 2,800 shi of red beans, 1,400 shi of sorghum, 2,000 shi of sesame, totaling 1,291,800 shi.

Changzhou 61

Bandit High School Student Escorted to the County for Interrogation: The Shangqu Defense Corps of the First District of Wu County captured Gao, a bandit high school student, and sent him to the Provincial Guard 3rd Platoon at Yang Kai Bridge for detention. At 2 pm one day, Cheng Jingzhong, the platoon leader of the team, escorted a platoon of soldiers to the city and sent him to the County Government for interrogation. County Magistrate Zhang personally appeared in court at 10 pm to interrogate him. Gao initially gave an extremely cunning confession, saying that he had not committed any crimes and had only two or three guns. After strict questioning, he finally confessed that he had more than thirty guns and more than two hundred accomplices. Yang Yaoda and Hua Hongxing (who had been captured by the Provincial Guard and sent to the county the day before) and Xu Genbao were indeed accomplices. He had commanded the bandits to kill more than a dozen people twice with guns at the Machouli Pan Shu Qiangmen and Machouli. He had also committed arson, kidnapping, and extortion in places such as Dingyan, Majiatou, and Jiagang, about seven or eight times. Although there were many other cases, he could not remember them. After committing the crimes, he knew that he could not survive, so he fled to Changzhou or Shanghai, and then to Zhaiqiao to sell soup dumplings for a living. In short, he had robbed people of amounts ranging from 150 yuan to 500 yuan to 801 yuan, and he had taken the most, etc. The county magistrate ordered him to be detained. Li Leng, the magistrate of Jiangyin County, learned that Wujin had captured the bandit Gao and immediately telegraphed the Civil Affairs Department of the Wujin County Government to transfer him to Jiangyin for interrogation. He also sent Fang Qi, the police chief of the county, to Changzhou with a letter to negotiate the reception and transfer. When County Magistrate Zhang interrogated him, Team Leader Fang also participated in the interrogation.

Yangzhong 62

The Baojin Isle School Rent Case Resolved: Since receiving the approval of the Education and Finance Departments to entrust the Zhenjiang and Yangzhong Education Bureaus and Zhenjiang Middle School to take over the management of the Baojin Isle school rent, negotiations with the county government to take over have been repeatedly stalled, causing delays until now. It is now known that the Education Department has fully understood that the case is entirely due to the former County Magistrate Xu Zusheng embezzling and disobeying orders and refusing to hand over the property. The Civil Affairs Department has been consulted to detain the former magistrate's secretary and Finance Section Chief, Qian Sui. Upon learning of this, the Zhenjiang Education Bureau sent Section Chief Xue Zhenglin and others to Yangzhong to join the Yangzhong Education Bureau to take over the property. Negotiations have now been finalized, and the formal takeover will take place on the afternoon of the first day. The Baojin Isle school rent issue, which has been delayed for more than a year, can be said to be completely resolved.

Hangzhou 63

The Finance Department Establishes Short-Term Loans: The Zhejiang Provincial Government, due to insufficient local revenue to cover expenditures, borrowed a large sum of money from banks and money shops for assistance. The previously rumored 5.5 million large loan encountered problems midway and is currently difficult to finalize. Recently, the Finance Department borrowed a short-term loan of 1.5 million yuan from the business community, using the newly established business tax revenue as collateral. The interest rate starts at one cent per month, and 250,000 yuan is repaid monthly until the six-month contract is cleared. The contract has been signed and will be implemented from March.

Planning to Build Three Trunk Roads: The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau is actively planning to build highways and has already drafted three lines to be built in order: (1) The coastal line starts from Ningbo, passing through Fenghua, Ninghai, Linhai, Haimen, Huangyan, Leqing, Yongjia, Ruian, Pingyang, and crossing the Fujian border, about 900 li long. (2) The Hangjing line starts from the opposite bank of Hangzhou, passing through Xiaoshan, Zhuji, Dongyang, Yongkang, Jinyun, Lishui, Jingning, and reaching Shouning in Fujian Province, about 900 li long. (3) The Changyong line starts from Changshan, passing through Qu County, Suichang, Songyang Qingitian, and reaching Yongjia, about 300 li long.

Improvement of Alum Mining in Pingyang: Pingyang, Zhejiang, is a region that produces alum. Since merchants Li Dian and others jointly invested more than 300,000 yuan to establish a bureau for mining, there are now 25 alum kilns and more than 4,500 workers. Each day, more than 1,000 packages of alum can be produced. Each package is worth an average of 2.6 yuan, and the annual output value is about 900,000 yuan. The mineral layer there is very thick and of good quality. It is now known that the merchants are planning to improve the mining for the sake of development: (1) improving transportation, (2) increasing capital, and (3) using machines. Once a decision is made, the improvements will be carried out separately.

Annual Sales of Gold Rice in Hangzhou: In order to understand the city's food sales and the rice stocks of each store, the Hangzhou Municipal Government dispatched staff to conduct a detailed investigation. The result was that a total of 754,114 shi were sold from January of last year to December, totaling the 19th year. As of January of the 20th year, there were a total of 183,987 shi in stock.

Security Guards Capture Bandits and Rescue a Hostage: The Dongnan Sanyi River Security Corps in Xincang, East Township, Pinghu, learned on the evening of the 27th that the notorious bandit Liu Dexing was hiding north of Jin Si Niang Bridge. The detachment went to search and captured bandits Wu San, Zhu Baisheng, Hu A'jin, Jin A'wen, and Zhou Fengshi, and rescued Yi Guan, the seven-year-old son of Han Jia Miao Ding Shenghe, who had been taken hostage. Combined Record of Robbery Cases in Four Townships: On the night of the 27th, the home of Sun Liansheng, a farmer in the Xiaochu Sun area of the South Township of Xiaoshan, was broken into by more than ten bandits armed with guns, who robbed two boxes of clothing and 27 yuan in cash. On the same night, the home of Shen Zhenglin in the Hou Shen area was also broken into by five robbers who looted more than 100 yuan in losses, as well as five cotton quilts and seven chickens. When they were refused, they proceeded to loot and rob the new house of soft goods and miscellaneous items worth about 300 yuan.

The Shuhao Cloth Store Closes and Reorganizes: The Dehao Large Cloth Store outside Dongmen, Xiaoshan, has been losing money for years, with a capital of more than 34,000 yuan. The store is owned solely by the Shen family. In addition to using all of the family's property to compensate for the losses, it is still not enough to cover the debt. The creditor companies, including Tonghui Gong, Xiehe Yiji, and Shunjih, have waived the outstanding debts, and the store will be reopened with additional capital.

Order from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education to Urge Schools to Submit Income Reports 66

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education's instructions to Nanjing Middle School and other twenty schools: The case was approved in a public letter from the Education Funding Management Office, stating that the administrative income of various schools for this year has not yet been fully received and must be strictly urged within a deadline. It is hereby ordered that, as usual, the administrative income of various schools is deducted in two installments every year in June and December. Now that February has arrived, the expenses of schools above the middle school level have been issued up to the first half of December, and the actual elementary schools have been issued up to January. This office has not yet deducted them. Therefore, a letter is hereby sent again to request your department to quickly disclose the detailed amounts of income of various schools so that they can be allocated and deducted separately. Please comply with this for the sake of public interests. The report on the income from school and dormitory fees for the first semester of the nineteenth year has been repeatedly urged to be sent, and most of them have now been sent. Only a few schools have not yet submitted them, resulting in the inability to summarize and transfer the income, which has long been included in the budget to offset routine expenses. The Management Office has repeatedly sent letters to inquire, so it is appropriate to order your department to inform the head of the schools to comply with the order and send the reports within three days of receiving this document for verification without further delay.

Jinan Express News: The Shandong Department of Education has scheduled a meeting of education bureau chiefs from across the province to be held in Jinan on March 25th. ｜Announced and Implemented by the Citizen Training Council｜

The Citizen Training Council of the Shanghai Special City Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang issued a notice regarding the promulgation of district education association zoning methods and establishment procedures, stating that the Education Association Law has been promulgated by the National Government and forwarded by the Central Training Department for notification and the issuance of provincial, special city, and county party departments to guide the reorganization and organization methods of education associations. Now, in accordance with the district party department zoning methods of this city, the zoning methods for district education associations and the regulations on the establishment procedures for district education associations in accordance with the revised People's Organization Program are hereby promulgated for your information and compliance. This is to inform you. (A) "District Education Association Zoning Methods": The city is divided into eleven districts. Except for District 11, which is handled in accordance with the area under the jurisdiction of the Zhenru First Directly Subordinate District Branch, all others shall be handled in accordance with the area under the jurisdiction of the current district party department. The order shall also follow the district party department. For example, District 1 shall be the area under the jurisdiction of the District 1 party department. (B) "Establishment Procedures for District Education Associations in Shanghai City" (Recorded in the March 1st issue of this newspaper)

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau Seals Up the Zhabei Confucian Association 71

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau sealed up the Zhabei Confucian Association and its private academies set up to collect money under false pretenses, after verifying the facts. The original letter to the Public Security Bureau is as follows: "According to the repeated petitions of unqualified private tutors in this city regarding whether the purpose of the Zhabei Confucian Association is pure, staff members were dispatched to investigate the association at Xingjia Muqiao, Xin Jia Road, and Huo Yuan Lane on February 6th. It was reported that the association has a building with a stall selling books downstairs and a private academy upstairs. The private academy was previously sealed up by this bureau last autumn. However, the academy has been revived and has defied the order to set up a school while this bureau is cracking down on private academies. It also collects money under false pretenses. It was verified that Gong Gaoxiang, the tutor of the academy (the son of Gong Heting, the organizer of the Confucian Association), was treated sincerely by the staff member in the capacity of a tutor. Gong said that the academy has been registered with the Education Bureau and the private academy named Kongzi Pingmin Xuan Shu Jiangxi Guan has also applied to the Education Bureau for registration. He asked the staff member to join the association for a fee of three yuan per year and to pay tuition to become a correspondence student for six months. After graduation, the association would negotiate with the Education Bureau to exempt him from being banned. He said that his teacher Fang Shiguan and his friend Yao Minghui have a close relationship with the Education Bureau, but the public relations activities would cost a lot of money. He then showed the staff member the Confucian Association's propaganda brochure, which stated that they would set up propaganda halls to encourage people to learn to read and that propaganda members would help the people to establish schools, such as 'You Zi She Zi Di Ji Guan' and 'Tong Meng Li Xue Di Ji Guan.' It is verified that the association is collecting money under false pretenses. It is hereby requested to consult the Public Security Bureau to seal up the association and the academy immediately and to publish the news in various newspapers to prevent the tutors from being deceived." Based on the above, the Zhabei Confucian Association and its private academies are collecting money under false pretenses and should be sealed up together. It is hereby requested that you investigate and order your subordinates to execute the order for the sake of public interests.

Shao Lizi, the President of China Public School, Takes Office and Swears In 72

China Public School held its commencement ceremony and the inauguration and oath-taking ceremony of the president at the school's auditorium at 9:00 am yesterday. Attendees included Gu Shusen, the representative of the Ministry of Education, Pan Gongzhan, the representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, Cen Dezhang, the representative of the Municipal Government, Deng Zhenquan, the commander of the fortress, as well as Hu Shuhua, Chu Minyi, Zhang Shiyong, Wang Jingqi, Xu Peihuang, the new president Shao Lizi, the vice president Zhu Jingnong, and all the faculty, staff, and students of the school, totaling more than a thousand people, making it a grand event. The ceremony proceeded as planned. First, President Shao reported that China Public School was founded to resist imperialist cultural aggression and occupies a glorious position in the history of Chinese education. He felt inadequate to serve as the president of Zhonggong due to his talents and learning, and he also apologized for not being able to be stationed at the school full-time due to his official duties. He added that the unfortunate incident at the school was not the fault of any one person, but rather the result of a bad environment. The Ministry of Education sent personnel to take over and changed the college to a department. Some students may be dissatisfied with this. However, it should be known that learning does not depend on the size or name of the school, but on the pursuit of practical knowledge. Moreover, all citizens cannot exceed the scope of government management, and they should absolutely obey government orders. Otherwise, the students' mission to learn will fall into a great mistake. In the future, the students must work harder in their studies in order to contribute to the support of the people of society and the approval of the board of directors. He intends to find ways to add a college of science or a college of engineering in the shortest possible time, but at present, due to limited funding, he can only gradually develop according to the department's regulations.

A photo of President Shao of China Public School taking office (taken by Wang Kai)

Gu Shusen, the representative of the Ministry of Education, said in his speech that the recent upheaval at the school was deeply painful and that the waste of money and the abandonment of studies were even more regrettable. The resolution of the board of directors was not implemented during the upheaval. This stable phenomenon occurring in the highest institution of learning is truly alarming. The Ministry of Education has adopted decisive measures. It is a pity that the school, which has been carefully established, has been discontinued. Therefore, I was sent by the Ministry along with Mr. Cen and Mr. Zhu to take temporary custody and order all students to leave the school. This method was originally intended to give the students a chance to think quietly without any other malicious intentions. Later, the board of directors publicly elected Mr. Shao Lizi as the president and Mr. Zhu Jingnong as the vice president. Mr. Shao is an advanced member of our party, and Mr. Zhu is an expert in education. The future development of the school will be immeasurable. Yao, the martyr of this school, said in his will that "the mission of China Public School is to create qualified true citizens and talented people to save the times." In the future, I hope that you will strive to complete this mission and live up to the great hope of the founder, Yao, who sacrificed his life for the school. The Three Principles of the People are defined by the Ministry of Education as the core educational ideology. Students should study hard and sincerely embrace it in preparation for saving China in the future.

▲ Pan Gongzhan, the representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, said that Zhonggong has a glorious and revolutionary history in the history of Chinese education, which has been explained in detail by the government. However, it is a big mistake for ordinary people to think that opposing the government is revolution. It should be known that revolutionaries should engage in destructive work and resist the government during the warlord dictatorship. Now that the government is carrying out the Prime Minister's instructions and working hard on construction, students should earnestly study knowledge for the benefit of future generations in order to be called true revolutionaries. If they do not know how to study hard, ignore the needs of the times, and purely engage in destruction, they are not worthy of being called revolutionaries.

▲ Vice President Zhu gave a speech. Finally, President Shao answered and introduced Vice President Zhu. Vice President Zhu said in his speech that he was a member of the school who returned to China to resist the Japanese student regulations. He recalled that at the beginning of the school's establishment, most of the people in charge of the school and the internal students were members of the Tongmenghui, and the Three Principles of the People were embraced. Moreover, the students at that time were very autonomous. If they made a mistake, they would impeach themselves and never conceal it. In the future, I hope that you will do your best to preserve this glorious history and live up to the expectations of the founders for you to advance. There were also speeches by President Jiao Quanli of Datong, President Hu of Huda, President Liu of Shanghai University, and Mr. Liu Nanhai of the school's board of directors. The speeches were lengthy and will be omitted. Finally, photos were taken for commemoration.

The Establishment of Practical Vocational Schools 74

Gan Chunquan, a staff member of the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center, and Lu Yuanlei, the Director of Academic Affairs of the Shanghai National Medical College, considering the societal need for specialized personnel in Chinese writing and bookkeeping, have jointly established a practical vocational supplementary night school at the intersection of Xiafei Road and Hualong Road. The school adopts a course selection system and a credit system. Those who wish to study Chinese, bookkeeping, English, Chinese typing, or English typing can freely choose their courses. Furthermore, due to the credit system, students can enroll at any time and graduate upon completing enough credits, regardless of gender or age, as long as their academic level is adequate to pass the entrance exam. Recently, most institutions have been using Chinese typing. If one studies at this school, they can acquire the necessary skills in a very short period to meet the needs of society. Enrollment has already begun, and it is said that the number of applicants is quite large.

▲ According to European and American botanists, in recent years, the size and color of all flowers have increased much more than in the past, but the fragrance has decreased more than before.

▲ All waitresses in a large restaurant in London must undergo rigorous training. "Smiling" is also part of the training, because if they always have a smile on their faces, there will be no slow service.

▲ Two sharks, each 28 feet long, were caught near Swansea, South Wales. They are rare among sharks.

▲ In Ash, a village in Surrey, England, countless wasps suddenly flew to a man's shoulders and neck and gathered there. The man did not move and waited for them to fly away. He was not stung.

▲ The natives of the Brazilian wilderness have a secret medicine that they take before going to war. It is said that they can gain superhuman courage and can defeat ten enemies with one.

▲ In the city of Livato Ganaro, the capital of Brazil, there was initially a large mountain right in the center. In order to make the whole city prosperous, the mountain was removed using the high pressure of hydraulic power.

▲ Canada has a lot of water flow, so almost half of the world's water power is used.

▲ In Surrey, England, travelers often pass through by stagecoach and throw coins and candy to the children to pick up. If they don't report it, they will be caught by the officials and fined.

Explanation of Shangsi Festival 84

— Qing Qu

The two characters "Shangsi" are well known on the third day of the third month, just as the fifth day of the fifth month is called "Chongwu" and the ninth day of the ninth month is called "Chongjiu," all having the same meaning. Therefore, the third day of the third month is also called "Chongsan." Now that the old calendar has been abolished and the national calendar is followed, the good days of the past can be replaced. For example, the tenth day of the tenth month is like the refreshing weather on the third day of the third month. If we want to change customs, this "Shangsi" festival should not be forgotten. I believe that it should be recorded today and should not be lingered over in the abolished calendar.

After examining the character "ji" in "Shangsi," it is different from "ji" and "ji." Those who are illiterate cannot distinguish them at a glance. After careful examination, they seem the same but are actually different. "Ji" is read as yang li qie, meaning to have an end. "Ji" is read as ju li qie, meaning to refer to oneself. This is the difference between "ji" one and "ji" one, and they cannot be confused. As for the character "ji" in "Shangsi," it has a different explanation, like saying that in the third month, the yang qi has been released, the yin qi has been hidden, and all things have become patterned. Therefore, "ji" is a snake, and the image is shaped like a figure. Therefore, in terms of the zodiac, the year of "ji" belongs to the snake. This can be verified. Furthermore, according to Han Shi Zhang Ju, the customs of the Zheng Kingdom on the "Shangsi" day of the third month are to hold orchids to summon souls and continue the soul at the two rivers of Zhen and Wei, to dispel misfortune. The custom of "Shangsi" did not originate from the flowing wine cups on the winding stream during the Jin Dynasty. Wang Yishao was only following the rhymes of his predecessors. Moreover, since the Wei Dynasty, only the "third day" has been used and not "ji." Also, according to the rhyme supplement, "ji" and "ji" are not distinguished. Now, those with hooks are used as "ji" at the end, and those without hooks are used as "ji" at the end. The original meaning of these two characters has not been clarified. Therefore, this article is written to explain the "Shangsi" festival. As for the classics, I have already described them separately to avoid complexity.
