What I Heard About Gelao Lane 87

— Yingchuan Qiushui

Gelao Lane in Shanghai County is said to be demolished because it obstructs the road and is dangerous. This lane was originally built by Xu Guangqi, a Wenyuange University scholar in the late Ming Dynasty. Guangqi was a fellow villager and translated Euclid's Elements of Geometry by the Greek and had works such as Nongzheng Quanshu. From this, we know that Guangqi today is not only a pioneer in his hometown but also a mentor of science. The lane was built in the late Ming Dynasty and completed in the early Qing Dynasty, which is nearly three hundred years ago. Whether it should be demolished or not will not be discussed for the time being. However, I heard people say that Qiao Zhao, the Zhejiang Admiral in the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty, was known for his bravery before he was promoted. One day, a horse suddenly came in front of the county office and galloped east and west, and no one could control it. Zhao happened to pass by and chased after it and captured it. The horse still did not accept the reins. Zhao jumped on it and held its mane with all his strength. The horse became even more angry and galloped wildly. Zhao happened to pass under the lane and jumped unexpectedly, clamping the horse's belly with both feet. The horse jumped into the air, and Zhao held the horizontal stone under the three characters "Gelao Lane" and would not let go. The horse then lowered its head and dared not move. Zhao then let go and jumped down, and the horse was tamed like a good horse that was not worthy of his strength. The rumors are like this, but there is no evidence in the Shanghai records. It may be that Qiao Yiqi's story in the Wanli period of the Ming Dynasty was mistakenly passed on as Qiao Zhao's story. It is also unknown whether Yiqi once clamped the four hooves of a wild horse in the air. The story is seen in the Tongzhi Shanghai County Chronicle. However, Yiqi was before Guangqi, so it is inconvenient to put it together. Therefore, everyone mistakenly believed it to be Qiao Zhao's story. Wait for someone with extensive knowledge to verify it.

Anecdotes from the Hawthorn Case 88

— Zheng Yimei

My friend Cheng Xiaoqing's Hawthorn detective novel has been famous in the literary world for many years. Xiaoqing himself said that he did not write his life's detective novels to gain fame, but they are not as good as Conan Doyle in terms of quality and quantity. He has already surpassed Sherlock Holmes in terms of quality. The recently published compilation of Hawthorn detective novels is one of the crystallization of his hard work. Xiaoqing's residence is a small building with several rooms on the bank of Fengxi Creek in Wumen. He has the elegance of poetry and books, the sun, the moon, and the seagulls. He often walks alone in the suburbs and woods, often forgetting to eat while moving. He uses this outdoor scenery to conceive detective stories. After the conception is obtained, he immediately returns to the room to write a picture, from A to B, from B to C, D, and from C, D to E and F, which is the step of his detective stories. After the tortuous picture is completed, he tries his best, or between A, B, C, and D, there are still clouds and waves that can be described. Therefore, Xiaoqing's writing of detective stories is more difficult than any other type of novel. The most painful thing is to meet the book seller's request to limit the number of words to two or three thousand, which is not enough to write freely. Five or six thousand words are redundant and have too many superfluous words. It is not as good as the automatic writing, which is appropriate and accurate for each piece of 12,000 words. There is always an assistant in the detective stories, just like Watson and Sherlock Holmes. Bao Lang is Hawthorn's assistant. Zhao Zhiyan and Xiaoqing are good friends and come in and out together. The peers call him Bao Lang, and Zhiyan smiles and seems to have tacitly approved. Xiaoqing once worked in a certain department of Soochow University. A certain Western woman, a colleague, loved to read his detective stories and encouraged him to translate it into English to introduce it to a certain Western magazine. Xiaoqing also excels in Chinese painting. Many Westerners buy it and ship it across the ocean to display it in their country. The Taoist Western Line, my friend's front delivery is unlimited.

▲ Short dispatch The Nanjing Road China National Products Joint Department Store Recreation Department recently compiled a god and strange philosophical song and dance drama "Devil", which has now been rehearsed skillfully and will be premiered in the Juzhen Hall on February 28. The plot is bizarre, there are mysterious mechanisms, there are novel costumes, there are great sceneries, there are superb songs, and there are sensual dances (Yun)

Jiuyuan Note 89

— Chen Danyuan

The garden is named after hard work to record its labor. However, physical labor is not beneficial to the world. Yan Shili, the so-called labor of San Zhi, is probably moved by justice. He thinks about saving the world with his academic methods. He once said that if there is one person in the world who cannot understand his own bright virtue, then the bright virtue has not been understood in the world, and the world cannot be called peace. With painstaking efforts, I heard that I was moved. Mian Garden is located on the side of Taiyi Peak in Lushan. It is not in the world, but on the ground. Bitan Bright Moon, Mountain Bird Spring Dragon reflect each other. The essence is half a house. Seeking to hide the heart, even if the king is facing south, it is not enough to change it. The flowers and trees in the garden are abundant and uncountable. When the morning sun first rises, the distant view of the sea of clouds is crystal clear, and the waves fluctuate, as if there is another world. 南洋 Travels (129) 90

— Spiritual Flower

That day, a stage play was performed in the temple. It was a Burmese play entirely with women dancing, their activity greater than our female roles. I saw them perform a puppet show, with bamboo and wooden animals dancing, the skill was quite impressive. Initially, two people performed an elephant fighting a tiger. Although the elephant was fierce, it was clumsy. The tiger jumped extremely nimbly, and eventually the elephant was defeated by the tiger. I don't know if tigers actually win against elephants. I guess scholars staged it with experience. A water bird swallowed a fish, the fish trying to avoid it in every possible way, but in the end, it was eaten. The struggle for power in the natural world is difficult to describe.

On the 7th, I read the English book "New Europe After the War" at the Pengcheng Hall, which stated that the Dutch colonies are 55 times larger than their mainland. Therefore, we know that the Netherlands' dominance in the South Seas is not to be underestimated. Also, the country is damp and without mountains. The nation even spends huge sums of over 100 million yuan, using machines to pump dry the seawater to build new villages, which can cover about 50 square English miles, approximately 300 square Chinese miles. Their great plan does not spare capital. Jingwei filling the sea, the Foolish Old Man removing the mountain, Westerners truly have this foolish sincerity. But you don't need to go to the Netherlands to see such foolishness. In Hong Kong, you see many workers opening mountains and filling the sea. A small mountain has already been mostly opened up, and a large part of the sea has been filled. Many buildings have already been built, which is the former sea. The best thing is to combine moving mountains and filling the sea into one task, simultaneously using the stones from moving the mountains to fill the sea and build houses and erect buildings. Today, not only has the mirage been realized, but also castles in the air have become reality. The ideals of the ancients have all become reality today, which can also dispel all sorrows of the ages. Then, abandoning the nation and abolishing soldiers to achieve great harmony and even becoming immortals, the ideals of the ancients will also become reality for later generations. It is really hard to say.

On the 8th, a friend invited me to take an evening stroll near the outer city. The desolate scenery was fresh and clean, far surpassing Rangoon, with many trees and small rivers flowing through the streets, no dusty roads. The docks and streets were all built with iron bridges and iron railings, so they were very clean and beautiful. Living here is better than in Rangoon. The businessmen were Indian and Chinese, and the laborers were Indian Kalla people. A park was desolate. Many large bats hung upside down on the trees to sleep, their size larger than crows, which I had only seen in animal science textbooks before. The South Seas is a university for examining and investigating plant and animal species and human races. Mr. Lin Chaoying invited me to watch a Burmese movie. Movie tickets here are cheap, with two annas and four annas being common. The two of us spent one yuan and sat in the upper class, watching a noble princess running away for love, encountering tigers, elephants, and large snakes. I felt that the jungle scenery of the South Seas was very lifelike. There was also a female ascetic fighting an evil demon angel, unable to decide. I felt that the Burmese people's thinking was more noble than that of Westerners. I also watched a Chinese film, its elegance and delicacy also quite commendable. This is probably the expression of Eastern and Western societies. Also, from the women depicted in Burmese plays, one can understand the female-centered view of life, which is absent in China.

Financial Gold Market Situation Slightly Better

▲The situation is still stable. Yesterday, March 2nd, the gold standard seemed to be turning bullish, but the situation remained complex. Qianzhuang Begins Sending Account Books 93

The Qianzhuang industry, both large and small, in this port roughly went to market after the general closing of accounts on February 15th. In reality, it is similar to not having opened for business. It has only recently been activated, preparing to start sending account books to customers' accounts, which is quite busy in the process. The time for sending account books varies among the entire industry. The earliest started on the 27th and 28th of last month, but many Qianzhuang and small banks generally delayed the distribution until after the end of the month (ie March 1st) for the sake of convenience in closing February accounts. Therefore, distributing account books was busiest yesterday and the day before, and the latest will be between today, tomorrow, or the 4th, 5th, and 6th. It is estimated that all will be distributed within ten days.

Wheat Market Bullish Due to Spring Rain 102

Yesterday, the wheat market opened in the morning with the price of foreign wheat rebounding slightly by three or four jiao. The market seemed to have stalled, but then, because the harvests in areas like Hangzhou and Shaoxing were expected to be poor due to rain and snow, the purchasing of standard wheat surged again, and the market picked up. By the afternoon opening, customer sentiment remained firm and purchases continued unabated. The outlook for forward contracts was particularly bullish due to the cold and rainy weather. Opening prices for each month rose steadily. Although short sellers tried to capitalize, the improved environment rendered their efforts futile. However, the current price of Australian wheat is as low as 4.3 taels, so it remains to be seen whether this will cause a drop in the future. The standard weight for foreign wheat delivery was previously set at 144 catties, but has now been changed to 140 catties, which will make future foreign wheat deliveries cheaper. As a result, March contracts rose four fen compared to the end of the previous month, April rose six fen, May rose five fen, June rose one qian, July rose nine fen, and August had no comparison.

Zhu Qinglan Arrives in Shanghai 108

▲Consulting with Various Charitable Organizations

▲Completing Relief Work for Shaanxi Disaster

▲Firmly Declining Position as Supervisory Committee Member

Philanthropist Zhu Qinglan recently presided over the emergency relief effort for the Shaanxi disaster. Last year, he entered Shaanxi three times to handle disaster relief. In January of this year, he returned from eastern Shaanxi and then went to western Liaoning to inspect the flood situation. On February 22, he traveled south from Pingnan to Haizhou to attend the groundbreaking ceremony for the Jiangbei Industrial Relief Qianghe project. He then took the Yongping Wheel from Haizhou to Shanghai, arriving at the Yipinxiang Hotel at 10 p.m. the night before. Yesterday afternoon at 4 p.m., Mr. Zhu went to the Renji Charity Hall to convene major philanthropists to report on the disaster situation in Shaanxi in order to complete the relief work in Shaanxi. Mr. Zhu is scheduled to go to Tongzhou tonight for some consultations, and he should be able to return to Shanghai no later than seven days. Various charitable organizations in this city plan to host a banquet for Mr. Zhu and discuss fundraising methods. Furthermore, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, Xu Shiying, Zhang Gongquan, Lin Kanghou, Wang Yansong, Wu Zhihao, and others, fourteen people in total, are scheduled to host a banquet at the Juelin Vegetarian Restaurant on Wengping Street, Sima Road, at 6 p.m. today (the 3rd) to welcome him. Invitations have been distributed to invite leaders from all walks of life in this city to attend. It is reported that the areas most severely affected by the Shaanxi disaster are Qishan, Liquan, Wugong, and Fufeng counties. Mr. Zhu personally visited these areas to investigate the disaster situation in detail and saved countless disaster victims. Yesterday, this reporter interviewed Mr. Zhu and asked him when he would assume his duties as a member of the newly appointed Supervisory Yuan's Supervisory Committee. He replied that he had been running around for various charitable causes for years and barely had time to rest. He really had no time to engage in other work and did not like holding empty titles without practical value. Therefore, he firmly refused to assume the duties of a supervisory committee member and had telegraphed Beijing to decline.

Yesterday Evening, Philanthropists Welcomed Zhu Qinglan 110

▲To Organize a Fundraising Association for the Shaanxi Disaster Emergency Relief

Zhu Qinglan, Chairman of the North China Relief Association, arrived in Shanghai with his wife on the evening of the 1st to raise funds for the Shaanxi disaster relief. Xu Shiying, Chairman of the National Government Relief Committee, specially convened a discussion meeting with philanthropists at the Renji Charity Hall on Yunnan Road at 4 p.m. yesterday and welcomed Mr. Zhu. Wang Yiting, Wang Hanzhi, Zhang Xianqing, Wu Zhihao, Lin Kanghou, Zha Liangzhao, and others attended. Chairman Xu Shiying first gave a report, saying that Mr. Zhu, Chairman of the North China Relief Association, had outstanding moral character and literary talent, and his handling of disaster relief was particularly hard-working and tireless. Everyone originally intended to extend a grand welcome for this trip to Shanghai, but they deeply regretted that they did not know the time of his arrival. Now, everyone expressed their welcome with the utmost sincerity and wished Mr. Zhu good health. Then, Mr. Zhu stood up to report the details of the severe Shaanxi disaster (the detailed situation will be provided in a written report by Mr. Zhu, which is not recorded here). He also stated that in order to achieve thorough relief, it was necessary to think from the root and come to Shanghai to raise funds with various charitable organizations in order to proceed from the aspects of work relief, water conservancy, and education, so that the victims can have the power of self-reliance. Zhang Xianqing of the China Jisheng Association also gave a report. Finally, Wu Zhihao proposed that, while Mr. Zhu was in Shanghai, a fundraising method should be determined, and whether the name, location, and organization could be drafted first today, and then a date be set to convene various charitable organizations and chambers of commerce, banks, and money houses, and major philanthropists to carry out fundraising. It was decided to name it the "Shanghai Fundraising Association for Shaanxi Disaster Emergency Relief," and the location was set at the Renji Hall. It was planned to be established today, and the organization would be drafted at the same time. It was also planned to host a banquet on the 1st, where Mr. Zhu would report on the disaster situation and show a Shaanxi disaster film. The meeting adjourned at 7 p.m.

City Police Chief Chen Xizeng Held Inauguration Ceremony Yesterday 111

▲Mayor Zhang Supervised the Oath on Behalf of the Central Government and Delivered Instructions

▲Over Four Hundred People from All Walks of Life Attended the Ceremony

The new Shanghai City Police Chief, Mr. Chen Xizeng, held a supplementary oath-taking ceremony at the bureau yesterday morning at 10 a.m. after taking office on the 11th of last month. Mayor Zhang, representing the Central Party Headquarters, supervised the oath. The details are recorded below:

▲Attendees: Central representative Zhang Qun, Central Committee representative Wu Bokang, Two Roads Bureau Chief Hua Weizhi, China Merchants Bureau Director Li Zhonggong, City Government Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, Post Office Director Qian Chunqi, Songhu Defense Corps Commander Li Yingshi, Shanghai County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, and guests Zhang Shouyong, Zhou Peizhen, Liu Shufan, Wang Yiting, Ye Zhuotang, Yao Mulian, Wang Binyan, Gu Xinyi, Wu Yunqi, Ye Huijun, Wen Lanting, Zhu Yinjiang, Huang Jinrong, Yang Hu, Liu Zhancen, Zhao Jinqing, Lu Bohong, Jiang Yi, Huang Boqiao, Shen Junyi, Hu Hongmu, Jiang Dingwen, Yao Zengmo, and foreign guests including Chief of Police of the Public Concession, Deputy Chief Inspector Jones, Chief of the Special Affairs Department Qi Wen, Deputy Chief Inspector Shiweiye of the Public Concession Judicial Engineering Department, and all staff of the bureau, over 400 people in total.

▲Oath-Taking Ceremony: (1) Music Played (2) All Standing (3) Supervisor Takes Position (4) Mayor Takes Position (5) Bureau Chief Takes Position (6) Party Song Sung (7) Offering Utmost Respect to the Party Flag, National Flag, and the Portrait of the Premier (8) Chairman, Mayor Zhang, Reverently Reads the Premier's Will (9) Bureau Chief Swears Oath (10) Supervisor Delivers Instructions (11) Guest Speakers (12) Bureau Chief Responds (13) Music Played (14) Ceremony Completed

▲Mayor's Instructions: This city is a hub connecting the capital, with bustling traffic and a mix of Chinese and foreigners, densely populated. In terms of its position, it is the center of national culture, economy, industry, and commerce. In terms of its situation, it is the screen and defense of the capital, a vital military town. The foreign concessions cut through the city, making it easy for thieves, bandits, petty criminals, and reactionary elements to escape and gather here. Therefore, the local security responsibilities of the police in this city are heavy and cannot be compared to those of other ports. Since taking office as mayor, two years have passed in an instant. I have actively carried out all municipal construction, hoping not to betray the entrustment of the Central Government and the expectations of the citizens. I have always paid close attention to public security, because it is the place where the lives and property of citizens are entrusted, and it is related to local security and stability, and the focus of attention of both Chinese and foreigners. If there is any negligence, how can I face the Central Government and my citizens? Therefore, I have been diligent day and night and have not had time to rest. The former director, Yuan Quan, has been responsible for handling everything based on the city government's policies and regulations for more than a year. His achievements are still good. Because he has other tasks, he has been allowed to resign. Director Chen has always been known for his decisiveness in handling affairs. He has a considerable history in the revolutionary process and is well-versed in military and police knowledge. He has served in Shanghai in recent years and is very familiar with the situation in this city. I have known the mayor for a long time, so I specially appointed him as the successor to the Director of the Public Security Bureau. Today is the day of Director Chen's inauguration ceremony. I would like to briefly state the following points of expectation: (1) Seriously maintain public security. Although the overall situation has been pacified, the reactionary elements from all sides have not been completely eradicated, and there are many thieves and bandits lurking and wanting to stir up trouble. Maintaining public security requires special seriousness. This is the first point to pay attention to. (2) Strictly train the police. The quality of the police determines the success or failure of public security. Without strict training, it is impossible to achieve perfection. This is the second point to pay attention to. (3) Strictly prohibit smoking and gambling. Smoking and gambling are harmful to society and are related to public security. Without strict prohibition, it is impossible to eliminate harm to the people and cold chaos. This is the third point to pay attention to. (4) Improve customs and habits. The Central Government implements political training, first to correct people's hearts. Customs and habits that are not suitable for today should be improved to establish the foundation of society. This is the fourth point to pay attention to. In addition, completing household registration, traffic, eliminating bad habits, consolidating internal affairs, and the police power issues related to road construction beyond the boundaries are all within the scope of the public security responsibilities that should be earnestly rectified and carefully handled. We are in this political training period and want to repay the party and the country by personally uplifting ourselves and setting an example to our subordinates. How can we complete the mission and live up to the expectations of the Central Government and the citizens? I sincerely hope that Director Chen will devote himself to the public security cause with his revolutionary spirit, be loyal to the party and the country, and be even more loyal to the citizens. I hope that he will strive for good governance and make progress every day. The mayor has high expectations for him. Encourage him!

▲Guest Speakers: (1) Central Committee Member Chu Minyi spoke of loyalty to his duties and defending the country with his consistent revolutionary spirit. (2) Xu Jinyuan, Chief of Staff of the Garrison Command, said that the military defends the country against enemies, and the police prevent reactionary villains from running rampant. Only by connecting the military and the police can the country and the people live in peace and work. (3) Wu Bokang, a member of the City Party Committee, spoke. (4) Ye Huijun said that he hoped that Mayor Zhang would retain the positions of officials who are loyal to their duties and remove those who are corrupt and engage in malpractice. Mr. Chen Yingshi's memorial tower outside Ximen stands tall, and anyone who passes by commemorates his great achievements in protecting Shanghai. The new director, Chen, is his descendant and should be able to fulfill his legacy of maintaining local order so that the people can live and work in peace.

▲Bureau Chief's Reply: Mayor, Commander Xiong's representative, Chief of Staff Xu, Central Party Committee Member Chu, City Party Committee Representative Wu, comrades, and guests, Xizeng was ordered by the National Government and appointed by Mayor Zhang to serve as the Director of the Public Security Bureau of this city. I know that my talent is shallow and I am deeply afraid of being overwhelmed. However, Chairman Chiang and Mayor Zhang have encouraged each other from Xizeng's past work and history in the revolution and have ordered Xizeng to shoulder this task, so I can only obey orders and strive to shoulder the public security task with the spirit of the revolution. The police are closest to the people, and are like a preventive drug in society that eliminates toxins and kills insects. Shanghai is the largest city in China, and society is very complex, so the diseases that occur are also the most numerous. Those who transport all kinds of drugs, the communists, and all other reactionaries, as well as kidnappers and robbers, all regard Shanghai as their general source. Therefore, the public security of Shanghai is not only a matter of Shanghai, but is related to the provinces along the Yangtze River, and even the entire country. If the public security personnel of Shanghai can work hard and fulfill their duties, they can at least reduce many hidden dangers in the provinces. The efficiency of the police is different from that of the military. The power of the military lies in destroying the enemies that have been discovered. The power of the police lies in eliminating the dangers that have not yet taken shape. Therefore, the duties of the police should be to work hand in hand with the people, share interests and concerns, so that the people will respect the police out of fear, and love the police out of respect. Then the force of the police can be said to be concrete and popular. Xizeng should preserve the achievements and scale of the previous Public Security Bureau, and dare not fail to work hard for the plans and progress of the future Public Security Bureau. We must ensure that the Shanghai police progress along with the progress of the municipal administration. In the future, when the municipal government's city center plan is realized and Shanghai becomes the first model city in the country, the Shanghai Public Security Bureau will also strive to reform and become a model police force in the country. This is the responsibility that Xizeng should fulfill, and it is also the responsibility that all members of the Shanghai City Public Security Bureau should fulfill. No matter how hard or difficult, we dare not fail to strive to complete our task, to live up to the expectations of the Central Government and the City Government, and to meet the needs of the people of the city. Xizeng himself is deeply afraid that his knowledge and experience are insufficient, and hopes that Mayor, Commander Xiong, Central Party Committee Member Chu, City Party Committee Member Wu, and all comrades will give guidance at any time. Today, I am very honored and grateful to receive the teachings of Mayor Xiong, Chief of Staff Xu, Mr. Chu Minyi, and Mr. Ye Huijun, and the presence of all comrades and guests.

Economic Director of the League of Nations, Salter, Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 112

▲To Enter Beijing with Haas Within Days

Sir Arthur Salter, Economic Director of the League of Nations, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning aboard the British mail ship Loyal Prince and stayed at the Cathay Hotel. This reporter made a special trip to interview Salter, but he did not wish to express anything as he had just unpacked his luggage and had not yet officially met with the National Government authorities. Salter's trip to China was at the invitation of the National Government. It is rumored that the purpose of this trip is related to the 100 million pound gold loan led by the League of Nations to China, but it has not been confirmed for the time being. It is known that Salter has represented the League of Nations in handling the financial aftermath of Hungary and Austria with considerable success, and has also presided over the League of Nations' loans to Hungary, Austria, Greece, and Bulgaria. Salter is a British national who has served as the Economic Director of the League of Nations for many years. It is now heard that he will retire. There have been League of Nations personnel invited to China by the National Government in the past, including League of Nations Deputy Secretary-General Avenol, Minister of Health Rajchman, and Director of the Labor Bureau Thomas. Now there are League of Nations Minister of Transportation Haas and Salter, who arrived in Shanghai yesterday, totaling five people before and after. Haas contacted Minister of Transportation Wang Boqun and others in Beijing and then came to Shanghai. He also stayed at the Cathay Hotel. Yesterday, he told this reporter that he was invited by the National Government to come to China and had met with government officials in Beijing and Shanghai many times. He will return to Beijing in the next few days to continue the contact. It is difficult to determine how long he will stay in China. The reporter then asked about the purpose of his trip to China, but the answer was vague. When asked whether it was related to the negotiation of the gold loan, he replied that he was not a financier and did not participate in it. The reporter then asked him if he had heard anything about the gold loan. Haas replied no. Haas is a French national and this trip to China is entirely on behalf of the League of Nations. It is now heard that Salter will enter Beijing with Haas within days to meet with the National Government authorities.

Six Company Jianglun Alliance Raises Prices 113

▲Shanghai-Hankou Freight Increases by 30%

▲Effective from the 16th of This Month

▲North and South Seas to Increase Prices on May 1st

Gold prices have soared, and the operating expenses of various shipping companies have increased significantly, especially the hidden consumption of hardware used in the ships. Therefore, all water freight rates on the Jianghai routes are being discussed for price increases starting in March. Those who have already increased fees include the Changsha line and Chongqing line in the Yangtze River, which have increased by 20% and 30% respectively. On the coastal side, the Shanghai-Taiwan line and Shanghai-Ningbo line have each increased by 20%. As for the most important Yangtze River route, the six companies Taikoo, Nisshin, Jardine, China Merchants, Sanbei, and Ningshao have jointly proposed a business alliance, so the price increase of water freight is also included in the alliance's discussion. A result has been obtained and the details of this matter are recorded as follows:

▲Increased Water Freight: The six companies discussed the increase in freight rates for goods going up and down the Yangtze River at the second meeting to discuss the business cooperation plan. The meeting concluded that gold prices are rising daily, operating expenses are increasing, and the wages of crew members and sailors have been increased twice. In order to maintain business, it is necessary to increase the water freight price by 30% of the original amount, as with other routes. The agreed implementation date is from March 16th. The shallow water fee, which was increased by 15% last winter, is still retained. Even if it is abolished, it will be discussed after the 15th. After the agreement, the representatives of each company unanimously agreed to revise the freight rate table immediately and notify the customers for reference.

▲Alliance Decided: The six-company Yangtze River business alliance has been resolved at the second general meeting. The duration of the alliance is tentatively set for one year. The six companies will mutually disclose their business: (1) Unified transportation rates; (2) No private discounts; (3) Eliminate the practice of customers stealing and reducing weight; (4) Actual receipts and reports; (5) If there are differences in opinion on the alliance, opinions can be submitted within 90 days from the tenth month after the implementation of the cooperation and submitted to the association for public discussion to determine whether to continue the alliance in the second phase.

▲Discussion Methods: The sharing method for the implementation of the alliance still needs to be further discussed by the six companies, because the number of ships varies, the business varies, and each has its own special advantages and disadvantages in business, as well as specially agreed transportation contracts. It is not as simple as the Shanghai-Ningbo line. The China Merchants Bureau has a unique advantage in the Yangtze River shifts, such as Datong, Anqing, and Wuxue ports, which cannot be occupied by foreign ships. Once allied, it is inevitable that the bureau will suffer losses in this area, so the bureau also proposed that it should be retained and not included in the sharing item. Therefore, the sharing method of the six companies requires a long period of negotiation and detailed rules need to be formulated as soon as possible within two months. The principle of the alliance has been decided for now. Except for the details of the sharing, it will be implemented first.

Page 14

▲Overseas Fee Increase: After the six companies resolved the Yangtze River alliance, they continued to discuss the issue of increasing water freight prices on the North and South Seas routes. Taikoo, Nisshin, Jardine, China Merchants, etc. all have dedicated shifts at Tianjin, Yantai, Yingkou, Guangdong, Shantou, Xiamen, etc. Now, due to the loss caused by the gold price increase, it is proposed to increase the freight rates on the above routes. It was decided on the spot that the export freight rates for the North and South Seas will be increased by 20-30% of the original amount from May 1st at the same time. The details of the fee increase will be determined at the next meeting.

▲Arrived in Jinan at 1 p.m. Yesterday

▲Continue Flying to Beiping Tomorrow

The China Aviation Corporation's Beijing-Ping aviation line has been in trial flight for the past few days. The company received a telegram from Nie Kai yesterday reporting the whereabouts. It is learned that Mr. Nie and Mr. Zhang flew the Tianjin aircraft from Hongqiao Airport and stopped briefly in Nanjing. They arrived in Xuzhou at 1 p.m. the day before yesterday for the night. Nie and others also inspected the airport. After completing this, they flew away from Xu at 9:40 a.m. yesterday and safely landed in Jinan at 11:40 a.m. It was originally scheduled to fly to Beiping today, but Nie and others decided to stay in Jinan for another day to improve the airport because the Jinan airport is still not perfect. They will fly to Beiping again on Wednesday. As for Tianjin, they will stay there again when they fly back. Because Xuzhou, Jinan, and Beiping all have airports opened by the Aviation Administration that can be used, Tianjin's airport must be opened separately, so Nie and others will stay in Tianjin for a longer time. As for the official opening date of the Beijing-Ping aviation line, it depends on the results of the trial flight. It will be decided after Nie and others return to Shanghai. However, the staff at each station, three in Beiping and two each in Jinan and Xuzhou, moved to their respective stations yesterday to prepare for business.

▲ And inspection of various departments

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry held its regular Memorial Week yesterday (the 2nd) morning. Inspection can be divided into domestic and foreign sections. Developing foreign trade is one of the General Manager's teachings, and inspecting commodities is the first step in that work, so the methods must be particularly precise to increase foreign credibility, and then the national economy will flourish. Our country's products, such as raw silk, tung oil, cotton, and tea, all used to occupy an important position in exports, but due to a failure to improve, they are now declining daily. In the afternoon, he returned to 23 Yuanmingyuan Road to inspect the bureau's silkworm seed inspection department (the bureau established this department at that location because the original bureau site was insufficient) and the leather grading matters that were just beginning to be handled, in great detail.

The Ministry of Industry Seeks Input on Industrial and Commercial Difficulties 118

▲ In order to find ways to help

The Ministry of Industry issued a directive to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating that after reviewing the files of the former Ministry of Industry and Commerce, member Xu Peihuang of the Industrial and Commercial Conference proposed that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce inform the entire country's industry and commerce sectors to list their own difficulties, gather them for research, and find ways to provide relief. Wu Jian, director of the Hankou Commodity Inspection Bureau, proposed that each chamber of commerce be responsible for informing each trade and guild to state in detail their business difficulties or successes, as well as their hopes for how the government could provide relief or assistance, and that the chamber of commerce present these at each meeting to promote commercial development. These proposals were all approved by the General Assembly. Considering that our country has a vast territory and it is not easy to know the actual situation of industry and commerce in various places, in addition to issuing separate orders, the original proposal is hereby copied and issued, ordering you to list the most recent facts and their difficulties and relief methods in each industry, without delving into empty talk or mixing in prejudices, and to quickly gather them together and report them, etc. It is reported that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce has already notified the trade associations of this directive and will comply with it in a timely manner for verification and forwarding.

Exemption from Tax for Cotton Yarn Exports 120

▲ Implemented from March 1st

Since the government implemented the abolition of transit duties on New Year's Day this year, cotton yarn and other items have been included in the consolidated tax, which began on February 1st. According to regulations, customs duties no longer need to be paid, and those already paid will be refunded. However, in the past month, the consolidated tax has been collected as usual, while customs duties are still being paid, which has already aroused appeals from yarn merchants and customs brokers. It is now learned that the Customs Tax Department of cotton yarn has received instructions from the Ministry of Finance to stop collecting from March 1st. If export tax on yarn has been paid as consolidated tax, then exemption from taxation will be granted in order to comply with the principle of "one tax per item," but customs inspection will still be carried out as usual.

Demands of Customs Brokers During Suspension of Business 121

▲ Exemption from Customs Duties on Yarn and Cloth Subject to Consolidated Tax

▲ Pain Relief Requires No More Re-Inspection

Due to the Shanghai Transshipment and Customs Brokers Association's feeling that the customs had stopped yarn and cloth merchants from paying "black corner" permits, the brokers were subjected to heavy taxation and repeated inspection hassles and dangers. They resolved in a public meeting to suspend customs clearance from March 1st. Yarn and cloth merchants have been greatly affected by their suspension of business. Although the customs and the consolidated tax bureau have reached an understanding, business has still not resumed. Shi Zikun, chairman of the Transshipment and Customs Brokers Association, went to various parties again yesterday to negotiate. In the afternoon, he convened a meeting of representatives from various trade guilds and the Yarn Mill and Cotton Cloth Association at the Qingyun Lane office to discuss the matter. Shi Zikun reported that the Jianghai Customs had received an official document from the Consolidated Tax Bureau stating that machine-made local goods should be subject to regular tax, and that customs duties would no longer be collected on yarn and cloth subject to consolidated tax. The customs has agreed not to collect it, but the inspection procedures still need to be followed, so the customs brokers believe that the pain has not been relieved. They vowed not to resume business until the goal of one-time inspection and no more re-inspection is achieved. Representatives from various trade guilds also expressed their agreement with the idea that the procedures were too slow. Next, the discussion turned to whether the trade should bear business tax by increasing brokerage fees. Representatives from various trade guilds did not agree, and the meeting ended without a result.

Party Headquarters Opposes the Sale of Housheng Yarn Factory 122

▲ Please Urgently Stop the Sale by Local Municipal Party and Government Agencies

▲ Then ask the Ministry of Industry to Prepare Funds to Take it Over as a State-Run Enterprise

The Guomin News Agency reports that since the news of the sale of the Housheng Yarn Factory to the Japanese became known, all circles have paid close attention. The Third District Party Headquarters and the Thirteenth Sub-District Headquarters of this city have also declared their opposition. Wang Yiting and Gu Xinyi sent a letter to the Guomin News Agency yesterday denying that they were intermediaries in the sale and saying that they had never heard of it. The declaration of the Party Headquarters is recorded below:

▲ Third District Party Headquarters (above omitted) I have read today's newspaper and have been informed that the Housheng Yarn Factory was recently sold to the Japanese Gongda Yarn Factory for 3.4 million yuan. Upon reading this, I was shocked and surprised. The Housheng Yarn Factory is one of the larger-scale Chinese-owned yarn factories. It has been established for a long time and has more than 20,000 spindles. When the government is making every effort to promote domestic industry, and the Ministry of Industry is even issuing 50 million yuan in public bonds to establish five major factories such as cotton spinning, selling a yarn factory that is relatively large-scale and has been established for a long time to Japanese merchants is self-contradictory, giving foreigners endless ridicule. In addition to submitting a request to the superior party headquarters to jointly stop the sale with the Social Affairs Bureau, the Ministry of Industry should prepare funds to take it over as a state-run enterprise in order to uphold the fundamental goal of protecting domestic industry. I also hope that people from all walks of life will unanimously advocate to prevent the infiltration of Japanese merchants who are invading our country's industry. This declaration is hereby made in the hope that it will be understood.

▲ Thirteenth Sub-District Headquarters of the Third District (above omitted) All newspaper offices should be aware that our country's industry is nascent, so the people are more than doubled and the money flows out. In the past 20 years, the Chinese people have tried hard to create it, and they have been able to slightly block the leaks. The weaving industry can only be roughly built. Since the end of the Qing Dynasty, it has been created and operated in various places. Since the European War, more spindles have been added, and the vigorous atmosphere seems optimistic. However, according to a calculation of the content, the national 4 million spindles are operated by our Chinese people, only about 3 million, and the rest are mostly owned by Japanese merchants. Since Hongyuan was swallowed by both internal and external forces, Baocheng was sold to Xihe, and Huafeng was also managed by the Japanese. Chinese factories are weak in capital and have poor technology. The weaving industry is largely monopolized by Japanese merchants. In recent years, gold has been expensive, and imported goods are unfavorable due to high exchange rates. This is the day when the yarn factory reorganizes its banner and sees the dawn again. It is said that the Housheng Yarn Factory in this city has 60,000 or 70,000 yarn spindles and more than 1,000 looms. It is only because the authorities' speculation has failed that they have not hesitated to sell the huge factory, which has been operating for a long time and is well-known throughout the country, to the Japanese Gongda Yarn Factory. The news is infuriating. I have already submitted a request to the superior party headquarters to stop the factory from selling and to find ways to help. The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau strictly ordered the factory not to transfer it to foreign merchants privately. Fangji hopes that the storm will subside and be reorganized soon. I heard that on the 28th of last month, a shareholder of the factory, Xue, led 20 or 30 Japanese people from the Gongda Yarn Factory, taking seven cars to inspect the machinery in the factory, and it was also heard that a draft contract had been signed for 2.3 to 4 million yuan to decide to sell it. These sad and mad capitalists do not hesitate to endanger the foundation of the country and make a crime for imperialism. It is difficult to count. It is found that Japan has recently been suffering from the industry in this country, and the gloom has spread throughout the country. It has long intended to transfer the spindles to China and to swallow the Chinese factories. If there are no traitors inside, its aggression will not be able to achieve the desired results. The Housheng shareholders, who have been paying tribute to the thieves and have other lungs, have millions of private property. If they have a slight setback, they are unwilling to maintain it. According to its economic situation, it is not at the end of the mountain. There is no way to save it. Even if they are unwilling to operate and work hard, they should also think about the country's lifeline and transfer it to the Chinese merchants. There are many rich people in the words. The government may have a good plan to replace it and maintain it. It will not even be sold to the country's actions to send the factory. This is what my domestic compatriots should sigh and hate and gnash their teeth. My division has been hurt by the scene and cannot bear the fall of the giant factory to the hands of foreigners. In addition to asking the superior party headquarters to save it as soon as possible, the people of all walks of life should be asked to rise up together and oppose it. The time is urgent and Lin Ying is overwhelmed with grief.

Preventing Agricultural Associations from Being Controlled 123

▲ Oppose the District Agricultural Association as the Basic Organization

The First District Agricultural Consolidation Association of this city presented a letter to the Municipal Party Department's People's Training Association yesterday, stating (above omitted): Since the promulgation of the Agricultural Association Law and the implementation of the Agricultural Association Law, many days have passed, but the organizational system of the agricultural association in this city has not yet been officially announced by the party and government organs, so the original farmers' organizations in each district of this city do not know how to end or reorganize. I recently saw in the newspaper that the Seven District Party Headquarters of this city has requested the central government to interpret the difficulties in preparing for the agricultural association. The points listed are all true and consistent with the association's suggestions. However, according to recent news, some districts in this city, such as Pu Song, Gaoqiao, and Tangqiao, have organized district agricultural associations. At first, I did not understand why they were so easy to prepare and I had so many difficulties. Could it be that the farmers in Pu Song and other districts have already been well-trained and know the importance of organizing agricultural associations? However, after investigating the facts, the so-called initiators are mostly municipal committee members, district heads, and local security officers. In this case, it is doubtful whether they will be able to represent the majority of farmers' wishes in the future. It is also heard that the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau is also planning to use the district agricultural association as the basic organization. When asked how to obtain the consent of more than one-third of all those with agricultural association membership qualifications after the initiation, there is an implication that it is not necessary to investigate all of them. In this case, the agricultural associations in each district of this city will inevitably be monopolized by a small number of local gentry. It would be more appropriate to call such an organization a "Director-Bao Joint Association" rather than an agricultural association. (It is heard that the municipal committee members of each district held a preliminary meeting to implement the Agricultural Association Law. Mr. Yang Xinzheng, a municipal committee member of Caojing District, said that the district's Bao can be the initiator.) According to the association's opinion, the organization of agricultural associations in this city, which is important and has a large population, should have a basic organization under the district agricultural association, which would make training easier and more popular, and the effectiveness of the agricultural association would be seen. If the above-mentioned situation is true, the 23 village associations, more than 1,500 members, and all farmers with membership qualifications in this district do not want any small number of gentry to control the district agricultural association.

In order to dare to express my humble opinion, I hereby submit this letter to the esteemed association, requesting that the organizational system of the municipal agricultural association be promptly announced, and that there should still be an organization of village agricultural associations under the district agricultural association to avoid being controlled by a small number of people. I humbly request your approval and guidance, which is truly for the public good.

News on Preparations for the National Cotton Production Conference 124

▲ Discussing Methods for Overall Improvement and Promotion of Cotton Production

Since the China Cotton Production Improvement Statistics Conference was prepared, it has been actively carried out for one month and has gradually been completed. As the meeting date is approaching, the various situations are specially recorded below.

▲ Letters have been sent to participate in this conference. The purpose is to connect the highest agencies in each province that are actually engaged in cotton planting, so that they can exchange reports on the national cotton production situation, get to know each other, and discuss methods for the overall improvement and promotion of cotton production and national estimation methods to meet domestic needs. Since the announcement of this news, letters from various places requesting to join have been exceptionally enthusiastic. Feng Zhaochuan, Zhao Lianfang, and Sun Yushu of the Agricultural College of Central University, Chen Yanshan of the Agricultural College of Jinling University, and Lu Bin of the Agricultural Science Department of Nantong University have reported their participation.

▲ Representatives from the agricultural, mining, industrial, and construction factories of cotton-producing provinces have been invited to appoint representatives to attend the meeting. It is now learned that the returned letters from the provinces include Lu Feishu-liang of the Jiangsu Agricultural and Mining Department, Fang Junqiang of the Zhejiang Construction Department, Zhang Zecheng and Hu Pingchu of the Shandong Construction Department. It is heard that the cotton planting area in Liaoning is very large, but it is controlled by the Japanese, so the Liaoning Agricultural and Mining Department has also returned a letter to the meeting to appoint representatives to attend the meeting. It is heard that the remaining provinces are also in the process of appointing them.

▲ Meeting proposals In addition to the proposals put forward by the initiators, the proposals from all parties have been prepared in advance and are now being sorted and compiled. The content of the proposals is roughly divided into (1) reasons and (2) methods.

▲ Representatives' reports Representatives from each province have detailed reports on the cotton production situation in their respective provinces. The content is roughly divided into three points: (1) the current situation of cotton production, (2) past improvements, and (3) future plans.

▲ Lecture topics The following have been invited to speak: Feng Zhaochuan, Shen Zonghan, Tan Yuezhong, Zhao Lianfang on seed breeding, Sun Yushu, Fang Junqiang, Lu Feishu-liang on promotion, and Zhang Xinyi and Sun Wenyu, Na Aisi (transliteration) on statistics. In addition, there are Ye Yuanding, Zhu Xianfang, and Chen Yanshan. The confirmed topics are (1) Shen Zonghan's topic is Discussion on Chinese Cotton Breeding Methods, (2) Fang Junqiang's topic is Rational Promotion, (3) Zhang Xinyi's topic is Chinese Cotton Production Statistics Methods, (4) Sun Yushu's topic is the Question of Maintaining the Purity of Cotton Seeds in Promotion, (5) Feng Zhaochuan's topic is Various Studies on Field Technology and its Preparation, (6) Zhao Lianfang's topic is The Direction that Chinese Cotton Breeding Should Take in the Future, (7) Sun Wenyu's topic is Methods and Implementation Procedures for Cotton Production Statistics, (8) Ye Yuanding's topic is China's Cotton Inspection Policy and Cotton Industry Improvement, (9) Chen Yanshan's topic is The Origin and Hope of Jin University's Cultivation of Million Cotton, (10) Na Aisi's topic is Methods of Estimating The Catton Income in America, (11) Lu Feishu-liang's topic is Agricultural Extension.

▲ Preparatory meeting period The initiators are currently scheduled to convene a preparatory meeting on the 13th of this month. It is heard that the Jiangxi Provincial Agricultural Experiment Station has also sent a letter to join the ranks of the initiators.

Representatives of Three Foreign Telegraph Companies Went to Beijing the Night Before Last 128

▲ The Final Contract Should be Signed This Week

▲ People in the Company Say There Will Be No Significant Impact

The Da Mei Evening News reports that representatives of the Great Northern, Great Eastern, and Pacific telegraph companies went to Beijing on Sunday night and are expected to sign the final contract this week. People in the company say that the new contract will not have a significant impact on the company's position. In addition to China's recovery of the auditing and sending rights, it is expected that there will be no major changes in terms of telegraph services. Even the apportionment of telegraph fees, based on current signs, the company may not be able to have a more advantageous position than before. Expanding telegraph services and increasing revenue, in terms of receiving and reporting telegrams, are still entirely under the company's control before landing, and only after landing will they be transferred to the China Telegraph Bureau for transmission. Outgoing reports are still handled according to banana processing. The original personnel will also not be changed.

Special News from the Maritime World 129

▲ Trial of the Xin Kang Ship Case The Japanese Yachiyo Maru of the Japanese Postal Company collided with and sank the China Merchants Bureau's Xin Kang ship in Chengshan Bay, Shandong, killing dozens of crew members and passengers, and losing 1 million taels worth of goods. Claims were repeatedly made to the Japanese side, but were rejected. The China Merchants Bureau then filed a lawsuit, which was accepted by the Shanghai court. After repeated inquiries from the Commercial Bureau, the first court hearing was held a few days ago. At that time, the defendant from the Japanese Postal Company did not arrive, and the court could not judge due to the absence, so the hearing was adjourned to a later date. Yesterday was the second hearing, and the China Merchants Bureau submitted a complete list of losses and a report on the accident to the court. This case is of great importance and cannot be concluded in one or two hearings. It is currently being heard.

▲ Naval Academy Students Set Sail The Naval Department dispatched students to England to study naval warfare and other academic subjects, led by the English consultant of the Naval Department, Mr. Peters. They arrived in Shanghai from Beijing and purchased tickets on the British Postal Ship Kai Fa to set sail. Today, the students will board the ship at the Gonghexiang Wharf. Previously, the Kai Fa caught fire in Dalian, and 22 second-class cabins were burned, causing great losses. The shipowner has now repaired the damaged cabins with cement, and will carry out major repairs after the ship arrives in London.

▲ Ministry of Industry Official Loses Son The Ministry of Industry issued a directive to Shanghai yesterday, stating: According to a report from Ministry official Ye Zhaochang, his son, Ye Guobin, who was studying at Aurora University, went missing on February 15 and has not returned home. A description of his appearance and clothing is specially provided, and Shanghai's wheel bureaus are requested to notify each wheel to carefully investigate and, if found, detain him and send him to Beijing. Ye Guobin is 15 years old, speaks with a Huai'an accent, is 4 feet 5 inches tall, has yellowish-black hair, and is wearing casual clothes. Yesterday, each wheel bureau relayed the message to each commercial wheel, ordering them to pay attention to the investigation.

▲ Continued Operation of Maritime Insurance The Shanghai Maritime Association, which initiated the establishment of the Maritime Insurance Company last year, has decided to dissolve due to insufficient subscription. The 4,000 taels of share silver received from Datong and other companies were returned by the Navigation Association yesterday. However, in order to take care of the interests of the crew members and sailors, eight wheel bureaus, including China Merchants, Sanbei, Ning Shao, and Zhao Xing, decided to organize a maritime insurance company separately. The share capital is recognized by the eight bureaus and underwrites the crew members and sailors of the eight companies. In the future, if an accident occurs, compensation can be obtained as consolation. Yesterday, Chen Bogang, chairman of the Navigation Association, invited representatives from eight companies to the Tongxinglou to discuss the progress of the establishment. Its charter is already in the process of being drafted.

Armed Drama in Front of Gaochang Temple 131

▲ Navy Artisans Beat Up Tram Ticket Seller

At around 10:00 AM the day before yesterday, a tram on Route 4 of the China Merchants Tram Company, which was heading from Ximen to Gaochang Temple, was passing Bansongyuan Road when it met a tram on Route 1 heading from Gaochang Temple to the Bund. As they crossed, eleven naval airfield artisans who had recently moved to Shanghai from Mawei boarded the tram. When the ticket seller asked them to buy tickets, the artisans refused, and a conflict arose. After Liu, the patrol chief of the Chenjiaqiao Police Station at Gaochang Temple, came forward to mediate, the artisans bought three-cent tickets each. At that time, both sides exchanged sharp words, and the artisans looked angry and seemed ready to resort to violence. Wang Zuocai, the ticket inspector of Route 16 of the China Merchants Tram Company, witnessed this situation and, fearing that it would cause trouble, followed the tram to inspect it. Unexpectedly, when the tram arrived at the Gaochang Temple terminal, the artisans were all standing in the tram and continued to argue with the Route 16 ticket inspector. A second conflict then arose. The driver of tram 30 also stepped forward to mediate. At this time, the police officer arrived on the scene, and the artisans began to get out of the tram one after another. The ticket seller of Route 70 and the ticket inspector of Route 16 then grabbed Zhang Likang, the leader of the artisans, and handed him over to the police officer, who took Zhang Likang to the Gaochang Temple Police Station and transferred him to the Naval Aviation Headquarters for review. A storm was brought to an end. At 8:15 PM that night, the Route 4 tram and the Route 1 tram of the China Merchants Company arrived at the Gaochang Temple station one after another. While the trams were parking, dozens of people resembling artisans were waiting to board the trams. Unexpectedly, when the ticket seller of Route 83, the ticket seller of Route 77, and the ticket seller of Route 108 of Route 1 got off the tram and went to the ticket pavilion to sign their tickets, the artisans wanted to retaliate and shouted "beat them!" They took out iron implements and began to use violence. The Route 83 ticket seller, Wang Quansheng, was injured in the left waist and internally. The Route 77 ticket seller, Chen Guanfu, was injured in the head and shoulder. The Route 108 ticket seller, Zhou Qiurong, was also injured in the collar and arm. Wang Zhifa, the driver of Route 69, and Dong Zhaoxiang, the driver of Route 83, and Luo Yunqi of Route 30 were all injured in the arms and waist. However, the Route 77 and Route 108 ticket sellers were seriously injured. When the company learned of the above-mentioned situation, it immediately reported it to the Second District Headquarters of the Municipal Public Security Bureau and sent police to suppress the situation. The injured six people were sent to the Shanghai Hospital for treatment. The artisans dispersed. Later, the company sent a letter to the relevant authorities to negotiate. After the tram workers convened a meeting, they asked the company to guarantee their safety and wanted to go on strike and stop traffic. Zhu Shaoqi, the company's traffic manager, repeatedly comforted them and explained that traffic was important and should continue as usual. The matter should be settled only after the court makes a public judgment. Therefore, the trams on each route still left the factory as usual yesterday and were all running. From 12:30 PM onwards, the Gaochang Temple trams only ran to the South Railway Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road.

Traveler's Suicide 132

▲ Impoverished and Oppressed by Economic Hardship

▲ His Letter to His Father Was Especially Heartbreaking

A traveler, approximately 25 or 26 years old, arrived at the Kaitai Inn at 422 Tianjin Road at the end of last month. He was wearing a fur coat and had a respectable appearance. He booked room number 26 and identified himself as Hong, with the given name Shanxian, a native of Hubei. He paid five yuan for the room. He went to sleep quite late the following night. Around 10:30 AM yesterday, he still had not gotten up, but groaning sounds were heard from his room. The tea server immediately reported this to the accounting room. They forced the door open and found the guest, Mr. Hong, lying stiffly on the bed, his face discolored. He was rushed to the hospital for treatment, where it was determined that he had ingested poison. He died despite efforts to save him that afternoon. After receiving the news, the police sent detectives to room number 26, where they discovered four letters. One letter was addressed to the deceased's family, and another was to his maternal uncle, Zhong Hengping, who practiced at the Yiji Store at 80 Ruilin Lane, Sanyangjing Bridge. Upon learning of his nephew's death, Zhong sent someone to handle the funeral arrangements. It was claimed that the deceased's real name was Jianqiu and that he was originally from Nanjing. The names "Shanxian" were likely aliases. He had previously worked in Hangaou but came to Shanghai after losing his job, hoping to find a new place to settle. Unfortunately, his plans did not materialize, leading him to commit suicide. Consequently, his letters contained expressions of economic hardship and various disappointments. The deceased left behind parents and a wife. His letter to his father was especially heartbreaking.

Letter from Chen Zhirun's Mother 133

▲ Too Miserable to Bear Reading to the End

▲ Chen's Suicide Was Due to This

On February 27th, a man named Chen Zhirun from Wuxi checked into the Renhe Inn on Xinmin Road in Zhabei. He stated that he was 30 years old and a merchant, but he did not pay the room fee. When the tea server asked him to pay, he replied that it was not yet time to pay. Because the inn had a policy of paying after staying, the tea server did not press him. After staying one night, on the 28th, he was found lying in bed, not getting up. Due to the issue of the room fee, the tea server went to check on him and found him foaming at the mouth and unable to speak. The police were immediately notified, and Chen was taken to Jisheng Hospital on Baoshan Road. He was diagnosed with opium poisoning and, due to the depth of the poisoning, was beyond saving. He died on the afternoon of March 1st. A letter from his mother, his meal bills, and four pawn tickets, and eight business cards (belonging to friends) were found by his side. Yesterday, Yan Liugen, the local security officer from Jiyitu, reported the case to the District Court. Prosecutor Wang and others arrived at the scene and confirmed that the deceased was wearing a Yuanbu lambskin robe and had died from poisoning. The body was ordered to be collected and the letters and other items were filed. The contents of the original letter, the menu, and the details of the pawn tickets are recorded below, from which the cause of his suicide and his conduct can be readily understood. The original text is as follows: The envelope was addressed to "Chen Xiaocheng, to be delivered to Huizhong Inn, opposite the Hekang Sauce Garden on North Zhejiang Road, Shanghai, from Wuxi County Machine Drainage Industry Association." The letter read: "Zhirun, my son, I know you are working outside, and your mother knows everything. However, is the work you are doing proper? As a son, you must do good work in the world after the age of sixteen to be worthy of being a human being. You must think about it yourself. You said you have a wife, but I don't understand your previous letter. You also said that the money you brought out has been spent. This must be my son's fate. However, you must always try to walk on the right path. What does your wife's family do? Are her parents alive? You said you had one hundred and forty yuan. Where did this money come from? Was there anyone to witness your marriage? After receiving this letter, I hope you will tell me everything in detail. At home, your eldest brother will be starting a business within ten days, hoping to be home by June, but there is still no business. I have been living at home for several years. People are constantly coming to ask for the money you owe. How can I face people? Think about it. The items you pawned may be overdue. This year, I may not even survive the new year. You mentioned in your initial letter where you were staying. Do you know that your eldest brother has to bear a lot alone, spending dozens of yuan every month? There is no firewood or rice in the house, just like when you were little. Have you forgotten me? Your brother does not know about the letters you have sent. Today, I asked someone to write this letter for you. Quickly find a proper job to do outside, and I can be at ease. If you do not listen to me, do not ever see my face again in this life. Words cannot express everything. I am writing this letter to inquire about your well-being. I hope your health is good. Is your wife with you? Another note: January 28th, 20th year." The pawn tickets showed that three yuan were pawned on February 16th of this month, eight jiao on the 18th, seven jiao on the 19th, and five jiao on the 22nd. The menu showed that he had spent seventy-three jiao and two fen on food. He did not practice frugality and was in dire straits, leading to this outcome.

Li Xiujuan Sues Zhu Mintang for Divorce 134

▲ Zhu Mintang, Young and Debonair

▲ Took a Dancing Girl as a Concubine

▲ Treated His Wife as if She Were Nothing

▲ Accused of Abuse and Abandonment

Zhu Mintang from Zhenhai, young and debonair, was a comprador for Arnhold & Co. last year. With ample finances, he danced every night and fell in love with Zhao Xiuzhen, a dancing girl at the Datong Dance Hall. When Zhao became pregnant, Zhu abandoned her, leading to her suing him for seduction at the Special District Court. After an initial hearing, a settlement was reached, and Zhao remained with Zhu as a concubine. She returned to Zhu's hometown with his parents. She gave birth to a son, whom Zhu doted on, treating his wife, Li Xiujuan, as if she were nothing. When his position as comprador was terminated, he ordered Li to return to their hometown, citing the high cost of living in Shanghai. Li proposed an exchange: after returning to their hometown, Zhu should sever his relationship with Zhao Xiuzhen, and Zhao's son should not inherit any of his assets in the future. Zhu could not accept Li's conditions, so she lived alone in Shanghai. However, Zhu never provided her with living expenses, and she faced great difficulties. Therefore, she retained lawyers Eson Ni and Ni Zheng'ou to file for divorce against Zhu in the Special District Court. The court session was held yesterday morning, but Zhu Mintang did not appear. According to the plaintiff's lawyers, the grounds for divorce, such as abuse and abandonment, were all based on the defendant's conduct in Shanghai. Therefore, they filed the lawsuit with the court, making the proceedings easier. The defendant should not evade the proceedings by failing to appear. Judge Yang instructed the plaintiff to postpone the hearing to a later date. Li attended the court with several girlfriends, but they did not know that the defendant would not appear, preventing them from confronting him. She was heavily pregnant and reportedly soon to give birth. If this "piece of flesh" were to be born after the divorce, wouldn't it be a fatherless child?

▲ Owner of Yuquanlou Teahouse

▲ Gao Shuanglin Still Denies Involvement

The Hangzhou Public Security Bureau recently apprehended a kidnapper named Wu Changgui. According to his confession, at the end of November of the lunar calendar last year, he colluded with others in the countryside of Yuyao County to kidnap a nine-year-old boy and hide him in the Yuquanlou Teahouse in the Qipu area of Shanghai. The owner of the teahouse, Gao Shuanglin, also known as Gao Xiaopijiang, was allegedly the leader of the kidnapping gang. Based on this information, the bureau requested the Shanghai Public Security Bureau to investigate. Chief Chen ordered detective Gao Wansheng to investigate and found that there was no place called Qipu in Shanghai, but there might be a misunderstanding with Qipu Road in the Public Concession. He went to Qipu Road to investigate and found the Yuquanlou Teahouse. He worked with Inspector Bai Zhongqi and Detective Bao Wang Qishan of the Huisi Police Station to arrest Gao Shuanglin, the owner of the Yuquanlou Teahouse from Yangzhou. However, the kidnapped boy was not found. Yesterday morning, Gao was taken to the Special District Court for investigation. Suspicious Death of a Woman by Hanging 136

▲ The Deceased Was Found Hanging from the Beam

▲ There Were No Tables or Stools Below

Tang Wenjia, a clerk at the Japanese-owned Fourth Cotton Mill and a native of Anhui, lived at 1795 Huade Road with his wife, Zhu. Zhu was 23 years old and also worked at the cotton mill. On the 28th of last month, Tang and Zhu went to work at the factory at 5 PM. At 6 PM, Zhu suddenly returned home and remained in the bedroom for a long time. Her younger sister-in-law and fourth child caught a glimpse of Zhu hanging herself in the room. They reported it to the police, who sent detectives to investigate. It was already 2 AM when the detectives arrived. They found the deceased still hanging from the beam, with no tables or stools below. The circumstances were suspicious. The body was taken to the coroner's office on Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo Huaipu from the Special District Court inspected the body. He took his seat and heard from the deceased's husband, Tang Wenjia, who stated that his wife's suicide was possibly due to losing some clothing and requested a coffin for burial. Then, Zhu Liu, the deceased's aunt, claimed that the deceased was forced to death and asked for a thorough investigation. Guo informed her that if she had any evidence, she could file a lawsuit with the court. He then concluded that the deceased, Tang Zhu, had indeed died by suicide and released the body to her husband, Tang Wenjia, after he signed a statement.
