New Regulations for Parking on Nanjing Road 139

▲ Effective March 9th

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Police Department issued a warning yesterday: "Please note the following newly revised Article 48 of the Traffic Regulations, which will take effect on March 9, 1931. No vehicle of any kind shall be parked on Nanjing Road for more than 30 minutes (except on Sundays and holidays) between 8:00 AM and 6:00 PM daily. Places where vehicles are allowed to park during this time are marked with white painted curbs. Places with red painted curbs are not allowed to park vehicles at any time. Furthermore, no vehicle of any kind shall be parked on the north side of Nanjing Road between 8:00 AM and 9:30 AM and between 1:30 PM and 2:30 PM daily. No vehicle shall be parked on the south side of Nanjing Road between 11:30 AM and 12:30 PM and between 4:00 PM and 6:00 PM."

The Issue of Collecting Seasonal Fees in West Shanghai 140

The Municipal Finance Bureau is now preparing to collect seasonal fees from merchants and residents in the West Shanghai area. It has sent personnel to investigate household rents and has posted notices. It is understood that the businesses and residents on the roads built beyond the boundaries of West Shanghai were once approached by the Municipal Finance Bureau to collect seasonal fees some years ago. However, the collection was abandoned because the merchants and residents argued that they were already burdened by the land taxes collected by the Shanghai Municipal Council (SMC). Now that the Municipal Finance Bureau is about to implement the collection again, the content and process of the SMC's collection of seasonal fees is attracting attention. The information gathered is summarized as follows: West of Haig Road, Di Feng Road, and Jiaozhou Road in West Shanghai is the Chinese territory where roads were built beyond the concession boundaries. Traditionally, residents along the roads and near the roads have used electricity, water, and telephones from the concession. The SMC initially collected a 12% seasonal fee from water and electricity users. In 1928, they began collecting seasonal fees from telephone users as well, and then uniformly increased the fee to 14%. However, those who did not use water, electricity, or telephones were not charged. In recent years, due to the needs of life, the number of water and electricity users has increased significantly, so the number of payers has also increased year by year. Even those who live further away from the road have been connected to electricity and are paying fees to the SMC. The receipts issued by the SMC state that the payments are made voluntarily. It is not clear how much the SMC collects in donations from outside West Shanghai, but it is observed that six or seven out of ten residents along Haig Road, Great Western Road, Di Feng Road, Connaught Road, Robison Road, Yu Yuan Road, Edina Road, Da Xi Road, Penang Road, Singapore Road, Brenan Road, and nearby roads pay seasonal fees to the concession. Furthermore, there are many foreign residents in the area, so the SMC collects a considerable amount of revenue from outside West Shanghai. Even as far away as Hongqiao Road, Sheshan Road, Beifang Road, and Robegen Road, there are a small number of residents who pay the fees.

Fei Deji, the Murderer in the Jealousy-Adultery Shooting Case, Apprehended 141

▲ Sun Changgen, Who Was Wrongfully Accused, Has Been Exonerated

Li Dazaozi, the owner of the Tongxing Teahouse at 355 Tanzhiwan, Zhabei, was shot and killed by an adulterer on the night of July 19th last year. The murderer escaped, and only Sun Changgen was caught. The Shanghai District Court sentenced him to 20 years in prison for conspiracy to commit murder. Sun appealed, and the details have been reported in the newspapers. Yesterday, the murderer, Fei Deji, was finally found by the deceased's wife, Zhao, and his cousin, Li Decheng. They took him to the Fourth District Public Security Bureau. During the preliminary interrogation, Fei Deji claimed to be a legitimate businessman and denied committing the murder. Zhao claimed that she had an affair with Sun Changgen before becoming involved with Fei Deji. Fei wanted to marry her as his fourth concubine, but she refused. Her parents arranged her marriage to Li Dazaozi. Sun and Fei harbored feelings in their hearts and shot her husband on the night of July 19th. She was working at the factory and fortunately escaped unharmed. Today, she and Li Decheng found Fei on Jiaotong Road and handed him over to the police. Li Decheng's statement was similar. The district chief verified the statements and transferred the three to the court for further investigation. According to another report, Sun Changgen, who was involved in the case, was acquitted by the Suzhou High Court after appealing and has been released from prison.

The Case of Seduction and Theft of 500 Yuan 142

Wu Shaotang, who runs the Tongxinchang Rice Store on Yangshupu Road, has an eighteen-year-old sister named Wu Maotou.

Page 16

On the first day of the tenth month of the lunar calendar last year, she was lured to the home of Chen Dehong, a bathhouse attendant who lived next door, under the pretense of playing mahjong. An hour later, after the game ended, Chen lured Maotou into the room. Chen's roommate, Li Shiquan, locked the door from the outside, and Chen forcibly raped her. Her mother found out and scolded Maotou. Unexpectedly, Chen then instigated Maotou to steal 500 yuan from her brother's rice store. On the third day of the same month, he sent Li Shiquan to escort her to the Sutai Hotel No. 24 in Suzhou to stay temporarily. When her brother discovered that the money was missing and his sister was gone, he knew that Chen Dehong must have been responsible. He reported it to the police, who arrested Chen. Chen confessed Maotou's whereabouts. On the fifth day of the same month, he, accompanied by police detectives, her brother Wu Shaotang, and Li Dean, who had once served as Chen Dehong's guarantor, went to Suzhou to find her. The police had previously brought a public prosecution in this case, sentencing Li Shiquan to one year and two months in prison. However, the 500 yuan that Wu Maotou stole has not been returned. Therefore, Wu Shaotang filed a private lawsuit yesterday, claiming that when his sister was apprehended, Wu Maotou had already used 50 yuan to have Chen Dehong make a leather robe. There were still 450 yuan hidden in the legs of two pairs of pants. Although the Suzhou Public Security Bureau searched, the money was not found. Later, when Chen, Wu, and others were about to be released, they settled the hotel expenses. While Wu Shaotang was away, Chen Dehong threatened Maotou, saying, "If you hand over the silver to Li Dean, otherwise, once you get to the Shanghai prison, it will definitely be searched and lost." Therefore, Maotou handed over all 450 yuan to Li Dean. During the previous court hearing, this was never mentioned or adjudicated, which was unsatisfactory. Therefore, he pleaded with Li Dean and others to hand over the money. Li Dean claimed that he had not received the money. Moreover, the detectives were present at the time, and the detectives who handled the case could be questioned. Chen Dehong not only denied receiving the silver but also denied having an affair with Wu Maotou. The judge presented the previous court testimony and evidence, and he had no choice but to admit it. Wu Maotou was then questioned. She confessed that it was true that she had been seduced and ran away by Chen Dehong. As for Li Shiquan being sentenced to one year and two months in prison last time, the three of them had colluded and agreed on the same story. They had said to me, "One person will go to court, there's no need for everyone to go together," etc. The 450 yuan was indeed handed over to Li Dean for safekeeping. At that time, Chen and others threatened her, and she was momentarily confused, resulting in this situation. She also pleaded for the return of the money. The court ordered Chen Dehong to be detained, and Li Dean was released on 500 yuan bail. Li Shiquan was still detained. The hearing was rescheduled for 2 PM on the afternoon of the 12th.

Electricity Outage in the French Concession Last Night 143

The electricity in the French Concession, from the Grand Clock to the areas of Avenue Foch, Rue de la Republique, and Avenue Edward VII, suddenly went out at 6:20 PM last night. It was not until about 7:00 PM that the repairs were completed, restoring the light and resuming traffic. Date of Dismissal of Shop Assistants and Methods 149

▲ Two Types: Contractual and Customary

In response to the question of the date of dismissal of shop assistants, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday sent a letter to the Shanghai New-Style Laundry Trade Association, instructing on the methods. The original letter stated: "Respectfully, on the 28th of this month, we received your letter inquiring whether the settlement date can be combined with the date of partners joining and leaving. After investigation, there are two preliminary questions in this case: (1) Has the industry signed a labor-capital contract? (2) If the industry does not have a labor-capital contract, has the joining and leaving of partners always been on the three festivals or at the end of the year? This aspect is what is called custom. Your letter did not explain the above two points and the term 'custom' does not seem to be appropriate and is difficult to understand. As for the inquiry about whether the settlement date can be combined with the joining and leaving of partners, the current settlement dates are at the end of May, the end of September, and the end of December. The dates of shop assistants joining and leaving are in accordance with Instruction No. 265 of the Municipal Government issued to this association on August 5 of last year, which stated: 'Approved the consultation of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce that the customs of shop assistants joining and leaving are different in various places and industries. After detailed research, it can be temporarily handled according to the old customs of various places and industries. However, since the settlement date of merchants has been officially ordered to be changed to the Gregorian calendar, the old time for shop assistants joining and leaving should also be changed to the Gregorian calendar.' This association presented this to the Social Affairs Bureau. Since shop assistants joining and leaving are handled according to old customs, if there are doubts about the period of joining and leaving at the time of the three festivals settlement, this time, according to the document of the Ministry, it can be changed to the end of May, the end of September, and January 5 of the year following the big conclusion at the end of December as the period for shop assistants joining and leaving. This refers to those who have not signed a labor-capital contract. Those who have signed a labor-capital contract, according to Instruction No. 2962 of the Social Affairs Bureau of last year, 'Contracts from the lunar calendar will be calculated according to the Gregorian calendar, delaying one month from the previous due date.' According to this standard, all labor-capital contracts that were previously set to be dismissed on the Dragon Boat Festival, Mid-Autumn Festival, and the fifth day of the first lunar month must be changed to June 5, September 15, and February 5 of the Gregorian calendar before they can join and leave. This association has presented a request to amend the two methods because they are so different and inconvenient. However, the approval of the Social Affairs Bureau has not been received. According to the above situation, there are two methods for shop assistants joining and leaving: (1) Those who have not signed a labor-capital contract are handled according to custom, but the date is changed to the Gregorian calendar. (2) Those who have signed a labor-capital contract, if using the lunar calendar, are calculated according to the Gregorian calendar date of the due date, delaying one month. This letter is to inform the Shanghai New-Style Laundry Trade Association."

Central Bank Inspection Report 151

▲ Eighty-Second Time

The eighty-second inspection report on the issuance reserve of the Central Bank states: "In accordance with the provisions of Article 15 of the Central Bank Ordinance, this association is responsible for inspecting the reserve of the Central Bank's issuance of exchange coupons. On February 28, 1931, the eighty-second inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of the bank. The results of the inspection are announced as follows: The total amount of exchange coupons issued is 26,574,112 silver dollars, including 26,100,8912 silver dollar coupons and 865,200 silver dollars of subsidiary currency coupons. The total amount of exchange coupon reserve is 26,974,112 silver dollars, including 23,500,9072 silver dollars of cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 16,330,780.08 silver dollars stored in the issuance vault of this bank, 2,317,017 silver dollars stored in the branches of various ports, and 4,861,274.2 silver dollars stored in the same industry. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 3,465,040 silver dollars. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank Exchange Coupon Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the guarantee reserve is 40%. The result of this inspection is that the amount of cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby made. February 28, 1931, Quan Fuxun, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Supervisors Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Ji."

Wang Bin, Shen Shifang and other two were elected as alternate supervisors. The meeting ended at 6 o'clock.

▲ Zhabei District Wood Industry Union held its inaugural meeting the day before yesterday. A total of 115 representatives signed in. Chairman Shao Shunqing reported (omitted) after performing the rituals. The constitution was passed, and officials were elected. As a result, Zhou Chengyuan, Zhu Yunqing, Hai Shanshan, Xia Yueshan, Shao Shunqing, Chen Lansheng, Zhang Yuqing, Zhu Hongbiao, and Zhao Rongqing were elected as directors. Chen Kunquan, Ye Shunzhong, Chen Ziting, and Cai Zhishan were elected as alternate directors. Tang Zhou, Min Yuncai, Zhang Jinqing, Lu Shunzhou, and Cao Guiquan were elected as supervisors. Li Fushan and Li Zhengshan were elected as alternate supervisors. The meeting adjourned at 5:00 PM.

▲ The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company No. 5 Wharf Staff Union held its 19th regular meeting of the board of directors yesterday. The resolutions were: (1) The executive committee of the Zhongzhan branch requested the company to urge the payment of the arrears of wages for August. It was resolved to send a letter to the accounting department of the head office, requesting it to expedite the payment. (2) The Mutual Aid Committee reported that Zhang Henghao, a member of the Zhongzhan branch, was confirmed to be unemployed. It was resolved to hand it over to the General Affairs Section to allocate 30 yuan of unemployment mutual aid fee in accordance with the regulations. (3) The Mutual Aid Committee reported that Li Shigui, a member of the Nanzhan branch, died of illness while on duty, and requested that he be compensated in accordance with the regulations. It was resolved to hand it over to the General Affairs Section to allocate 140 yuan of compensation in accordance with Article 3, Section C of the Compensation Regulations. (4) The standing committee member proposed that the registration matters of the organization section have not yet been completed. How should it be handled? It was resolved to hand it over to the organization section to handle it as soon as possible. (4) The standing committee member proposed that Comrade Tang Zhiyun's leave has expired and he should be asked to cancel his leave immediately to facilitate union affairs. It was resolved to pass the temporary motion: (1) Shen Youru proposed that this association was recommended as a publicity officer of the Aid to Holland Foreign Affairs Association. It was resolved to send a letter of resignation.

▲ The Steamboat Wood Industry Preparatory Committee held its second preparatory meeting yesterday. Ye Xianggao chaired the meeting and performed the rituals. After the chairman reported on the progress of the preparatory work, the following proposals were made: (1) The rules of the Preparatory Committee were adopted and resolved to pass. (2) The deadline for registration was resolved to complete the registration before March 4. (3) It was resolved to appoint Jiang Xuexian to be responsible for drafting the constitution. (4) It was resolved to reserve the date for the founding meeting and wait for the decision of the third preparatory meeting. (5) The date of the third preparatory meeting was set for 2:00 PM on March 4th. The meeting adjourned.

▲ The Third Special District Cigarette Industry Union held its inaugural meeting the day before yesterday at the grand auditorium of the Huacheng Cigarette Factory Union. More than 200 representatives from various cigarette factories attended. The presidium consisted of Zhou Haoyuan, Yu Jiasheng, and Shi Pinchao. After performing the rituals: (1) The chairman reported the purpose of the meeting. (2) The representatives of the higher authorities gave speeches. (3) The constitution was passed. (4) The declaration of the conference and the letter to the workers were passed. (5) The officials were elected. As a result, Zhou Haoyuan, Shi Pinchao, Luo Jikang, Zhou Lisheng, Wang Ruixiang, Hu A'jin, Lu A'ru, Wang A'yi, and Ying Yonghe were elected as directors. Han Azhu and Gui Fusheng were elected as alternate supervisors. (6) After taking the photo, the branch office cadres of each factory will continue to be held to establish branch office cadres of each factory. After the election, the meeting adjourned.

Weather Report 161

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday: "The Yangtze River basin and the coast here are cloudy, with fog or rain and cyclones due to the low pressure in Jiangxi moving to the east-northeast. The wind on the coast of Shandong and the East China Sea is strong and undirected." Also, the highest temperature in this city within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday was 44.4 degrees, and the lowest was 35.1 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 74.7 degrees and the lowest was 49.1 degrees. Letter:

To the Editor,

After reading your newspaper's Shanghai news column on March 1, which contained a section on the aftermath of the Gongfa Company's problems, my conversation was slightly different from the facts. I certainly had the idea of ​​soliciting people to lease the Great World and using the annual rental income to repay the creditors. As for other businesses of Gongfa Company, I was not clear about the content, such as the 50,000 yuan for the hot spring bath and the 300,000 yuan for the Chinese and Western pharmacies, etc. In the conversation at that time, it may have been a mistake to refer to the total rental price for several years. Corresponding letter, I hope to correct it.

Sincerely,

Min Caizhang

March 2nd,

Respectfully, after checking the land used for Beihui Road in our county at that time, the calculated land price was originally based on a width of 12 meters as the standard. Now the construction of the road only uses 9 meters or so. The remaining land on both sides is for future expansion. And in the Shanghai news column of your newspaper on March 2, there was a statement about our bureau setting up the boundary of Beihui Road, saying that the calculated land used for the road was originally based on a width of 9 meters as the standard, and now only 7 meters or so is used. The recorded number of feet is completely inconsistent with the facts. In order to provide accurate information, we would like to ask your newspaper to correct it quickly to avoid misunderstanding.

Sincerely,

Shanghai County Construction Bureau

March 2nd

Shanghai Market

Market News 162

▲ Qingyise Restaurant at the intersection of Sanma Road and Zhejiang Road declares that it has recently hired a famous chef, Mr. Luo, who has the most experience in frying and cooking. It is said that Mr. Luo has been engaged in the catering business since he was a child. When he was young, he was in charge of the kitchen affairs of the Guangdong West Hao Hotel. He used to travel to Shanghai, Nanjing, Beiping and Yokohama, all as head chefs. Therefore, he is indeed superior to others in food preparation and cooking, and many people in the industry also admire him. The owner of Qingyise is a close friend of Mr. Luo. He had once hired him before, but Mr. Luo's contract in Yokohama was not over and he could not come to Shanghai. Now, the owner, admiring Mr. Luo's skills, sent several telegrams inviting him. Mr. Luo, because of his friendship, could not refuse, so he came to Shanghai a month ago and took up the position of head chef of the restaurant. It is said that he has made many contributions to various special new dishes.

▲ Sanxing Candy and Tea Food Store at the intersection of Chongqing Road and Daqian Road declares that this store sells Zhenjiang aged vinegar, Yangzhou pickles and other items, all of which are famous local products from the mainland. All walks of life are welcome to visit. Wholesale prices are extremely cheap.

▲ Kaixuan Socks Factory declares that the fineness of socks depends on the density of the knitting needles. Kaixuan silk stockings have as many as 42 to 48 stitches per inch. The weight of silk stockings is directly proportional to the number of threads combined into a line. Silk stockings also have raw dyeing and cooked dyeing. Raw dyeing means that the silk is already colored before weaving, and cooked dyeing means dyeing after weaving. The former is more expensive. Kaixuan silk stockings are all raw dyed.

▲ Xinxin Flag Company declares that recently, a famous artist and a prominent figure in the business community have founded Xinxin Art Flag Company at No. 237 Jingxingli, Avenue Edward VII, skillfully making various flags. All color schemes, tailoring, and lettering contain beautiful ideas. At the beginning of the opening, low prices are promoted.

▲ Dahua Film Advertising Company at No. 2 Jiujiang Road declares that since the announcement of the company's invention of mobile advertising, dozens of manufacturers have come to commission advertising. It can be seen that this initiative is indeed a new force in publicity. The first publicity team has already set off at the end of last month.

Publishing News 163

▲ The China Women's Temperance Association, Room 508, 5th Floor, No. 3 Niansan Road, Yuanmingyuan Road, declares that the Temperance Monthly, edited by the association, Volume 9, Issue 10, was published the day before yesterday. The main items are A Short History of the China Women's Temperance Association, Ms. Shi Yunying's On the Footing of Temperance Sees the Life of Nanjing Women, Ms. Bingxue's Prostitution and Venereal Diseases in Jiangsu Province, Ms. Yang Meizhen's Temperance is a Tool for Saving the Country, Ms. Jingxiu's The Corruption of Our Country's Family Education and its Remedy, the content is rich, and it is not possible to list them in detail. Those who want to buy can go to the editorial department of this association, and mail orders only need to attach a one-dime stamp.

Recent News from the Modern Reading Club 164

The Modern Reading Club on Sima Road has achieved remarkable success since its establishment. The number of members has reached over one thousand households. The publishing house is preparing three types of publications. One, the *Avant-Garde Monthly*, has already been published, with sales exceeding ten thousand copies. Two others, *Modern Literature and Art* and *Dramatic Movement*, are announced for imminent publication. It is now heard that *Dramatic Movement* has been renamed *Modern Literary Criticism*, with Li Zanhua, the chief editor of the publishing house, taking on the role of editor-in-chief. The first special large issue is scheduled for publication on April 10th. The content is divided into various sections, including: Special Essays on Literature from Various Countries, Research on Writers from Various Countries, Introductions to World Masterpieces, World Literary News, Literary Anecdotes, Translation Commercial School, Writer News, and Publication News. It will also publish as many novels, dramas, poems, and essays as possible, with each issue containing approximately 150,000 words. Long-term contributors include Chuan Donghua, Xie Liuyi, Zhao Jingshen, Xu Weinan, Ye Lingfeng, Mu Bentian, Shen Congwen, Sun Lianggong, Sun Xiling, Yu Xiuyun, Shen Qiyu, Lin Yijin, Shao Guanhua, and more than forty others, which can be described as an unprecedented grand gathering of Chinese literary and artistic writers. All members of the Modern Reading Club are entitled to a free half-year subscription (choosing one of the three publications). It is expected that the publication of this journal will create a sensation in the literary world.

Dawn Bookstore Opens a New Retail Department 165

Since its opening, the Dawn Bookstore has seen considerable development in its business. With the increasing number of books published and the continuous stream of purchases from various schools, it became necessary to establish a retail department. A new retail department has been specially set up at the intersection of Sima Road, Zhongshi Wangping Street, next to the New Moon Bookstore, inside the Masses Bookstore Company. It officially started business on March 1st. The location is central and convenient for transportation, which will greatly facilitate the purchase of books for people from all walks of life. It is said that the general office of the bookstore is still located in Dade Lane, South Chengdu Road.

Publication of "Era Youth" Issue 27 166

*Era Youth*, published by the Era Youth Society, has been highly praised in youth circles since its publication. The journal has expanded its original format starting with the 27th issue. This issue was published on March 1st. The main contents include "Youth and Politics," "The Status of Modern Women under Capitalism and Their Due Awareness," "Prospects for Recovering the Shanghai Concessions and Revolutionary Diplomacy," "Youth and Reading Clubs," "Relief for the Crisis of School Dropout during the Period of Transformation," "Mute Ambition" (a novel), and "School Without Wire Electricity," which are even more exciting than the previous issues. In addition to the major bookstores that sell it, news vendors and school gatehouses also have sales outlets. Each copy costs three cents, and a full year's subscription including postage costs one dollar and sixty cents.

Reader's Letter 167

I would like to request a copy of this newspaper's *Art Section* from December 15th of last year. Readers who are willing to provide it will be rewarded with a copy of a new novel. First come, first served. Send the item to: Chu Anping, Guanghua University, Shanghai.

Notice from the Shanghai Market Editorial Department 168

(1) Please specify "Shanghai Market Department Received" when sending manuscripts from businesses, doctors, film companies, theaters, calligraphers, and painters.

(2) Please affix a seal for verification when sending manuscripts from businesses, film companies, theaters, calligraphers, painters, and doctors, otherwise, we regret that we will not publish them.

(3) Regarding lengthy manuscripts on film matters, we will continue our past practice of offering a small honorarium, calculated at one yuan per thousand words.
